However, the official decision will probably be announced after Simon and Eden return from Berlin early next week. British Four-Year Plan to Expand Air Force 29

Budget Increases Sharply, Total Strength Expected to Reach 100.5 Squadrons

Far East Route Planned to Extend to Hong Kong via Australia and Siam

[London] The British Air Force budget estimates stipulate that the British Air Force will increase by 40.5 squadrons by the end of 1938. From this, it can be seen that Britain is determined to expand its air force strength to be equal to that of the French Air Force. The Air Force budget totals 23,811,000 pounds, an increase of 3,685,000 pounds compared to 1934, including the additional funding approved by Parliament last summer of 200,000 pounds for the Air Force and 150,000 pounds for the Navy to purchase aircraft. The four-year plan set by the government will give Britain a total of 1,330 aircraft in the first line of defense. In addition, there are 130 aircraft incorporated into non-standby squadrons. It is planned to add eleven new squadrons to the National Defense Air Force, reaching a total of 54 squadrons, of which 41 squadrons are regular squadrons and the rest are auxiliary squadrons. The number of naval aircraft will also increase greatly. Including naval aircraft, the total strength of the British Air Force will increase to 100.5 squadrons. A memorandum on this matter stated that it is hoped that the air route from Australia to Bangkok will soon be extended to Hong Kong, and preparations have begun. The Hong Kong government has agreed to donate part of the funding. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

France and the United States Express Sympathy 30

[London] The British national defense white paper explained that Britain could no longer safely delay expanding its naval, land, and air forces, and France and the United States have responded to it sympathetically today. Responsible parties in Paris believe that the publication of this article by Britain at this time has two meanings: (1) British Foreign Secretary Simon is about to visit Berlin; (2) It is in line with France's steps, knowing that French Prime Minister Flandin will propose a two-year military service bill. US authorities also expressed sympathetic attention to this white paper. The budgets of the US Army and Navy have been fully approved and increased by Congress. Although there is no formal criticism yet, US official circles clearly acknowledge that the current situation in Europe provides a reason for Britain to increase its national defense strength. Berlin and Rome have not yet issued comments. German official circles are temporarily not expressing opinions, and German newspapers have not mentioned the white paper. Reuters' Rome correspondent learned that the Italian government is currently not prepared to make any statement on this matter. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

German Public Opinion is Agitated 31

[Berlin] German newspapers published and criticized the British white paper. The National Socialist Party's organ said that Britain is using the self-defense plans of disarmed countries as an excuse to greatly increase its military preparations. What is particularly noteworthy in the white paper is that it repeatedly mentions Germany and its military spirit, while not saying a word about Russia, which is vigorously proceeding with rearmament. At a time when the British Foreign Secretary is about to visit Germany, Germany is striving to avoid events that could cause difficulties because important negotiations are about to begin, while Britain seems to want to consolidate its position before the negotiations begin. The Essen National Daily News, which has close ties with Prime Minister Goering, said that the British white paper implies that the Rhine is the British border, which shows that Britain wants to regard Germany as its natural enemy. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

British Newspapers Offer Mixed Praise and Criticism 32

[London] British newspapers today are all criticizing the government's white paper on national defense, with mixed praise and criticism. According to the opinion of political visitors, the government intends to have a five-year plan to renovate the navy, army, and greatly increase the air force, and the national defense expenditure will increase by approximately 60 million pounds. Lord Snowden criticized this article, saying that it was the biggest tragedy since the European War. When he first saw it, he suspected that it was drafted by the French Foreign Ministry. We are actually implicitly treating Germany as an enemy. Britain's obedience to France has already led to one war, and now it will lead us into another war. The Huibao newspaper stated that the Labor Party will file an impeachment motion against the government because of this matter. It is feared that Germany will not welcome Simon after the white paper is published, and Simon's mission to Germany will also fail. The Times published a long article, defending the government with great effort. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Three Reasons for Strengthening National Defense 33

[London] The declaration submitted to the newspapers today by the British government is an important document on the defense policy of Britain and the British Empire. The declaration first states the motives for British defense policy, divided into three items:

(1) Britain has repeatedly devoted itself to the cause of peace, such as supporting the League of Nations, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, the Washington Treaty, the Locarno Treaty, and the Anglo-French London Agreement of February 3. Britain has not failed to support and participate in all of these. However, to think that various treaties alone are sufficient to guarantee peace is still premature, because the current international peace system has insufficient effectiveness in protecting countries from aggression. (2) Currently, countries are competing to increase their military preparations, especially Germany. If Germany's rearmament continues in its current state, it will inevitably be more difficult for Germany's neighbors to rest easy, and there is a risk of peace being threatened. (3) The protection of Britain's defense organization and the communication routes of the Empire has not been sufficiently strengthened. Protecting the maritime communications of the British Empire in wartime, preventing the lack of domestic supplies, and protecting the British people from aerial attacks are currently insufficient.

Based on the above three reasons, the British government believes that it is necessary to find ways to strengthen the defense of Britain and the British Empire. The declaration lists the scope of defense needs and the general procedures for increasing defense, divided into the navy, army, and air force, as summarized below:

(1) Navy

Battleships have always occupied a major position in the British naval strategy. Britain's current battleships are very old and new ships should be built and replaced in a very short period of time. The various naval bases of the British Empire must be developed and their defenses increased.

(2) Army

It is advocated to increase funding so that the army's air defense equipment can be greatly expanded. All army equipment should be greatly renovated to modernize it.

(3) Air Force

The progress of aviation technology has made the British coast threatened by air force attacks. Therefore, from the perspective of air defense, the territorial integrity of certain territories outside the English Channel is more important to British security now than it was in the past. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

[London] This morning, the government issued a declaration explaining the reasons for increasing army expenditures and the number of troops. [London] Today in the House of Commons, the Labor Party opposed the government's white paper on national defense, published in the name of a nationally united government. He only knew the name "British Government" and had never heard of any mention in official documents of the current government being a Labor, Conservative, or Liberal Party government. Roosevelt Advocates Direct Subsidies for the Shipping Industry 38

Abolish the Existing System of Mail Delivery Contracts

Commercial Use in Peacetime, Assistance to the Navy in Wartime

Message to Congress Lists Three Major Reasons

[Washington] President Roosevelt sent a special message to Congress today, advocating that the government maintain a sufficient merchant fleet with direct subsidies and abolish the existing system of mail delivery contracts for foreign mail. President Roosevelt said that the United States currently pays 30 million yuan for mail delivery contracts, but the actual price is only 3 million yuan based on ordinary freight rates, so the difference of 27 million yuan is simply a subsidy. President Roosevelt listed three major reasons, asking Congress to accept his proposal: (1) Peacetime shipping subsidies and other restrictions or rebate measures given by other countries can be used to destroy American shipping merchants. Even for the sake of maintaining fair competition, American merchant ships must have sufficient tonnage to properly operate American foreign trade. (2) When there is a war in other countries that does not involve the United States, American commerce will be greatly affected if it does not have sufficient merchant ships, because it will fail to find ships to operate neutral and peaceful foreign trade. (3) When there is a war involving the United States, American merchant ships are especially needed, not only for use as auxiliary naval vessels, but also for maintaining necessary commerce with other countries. President Roosevelt also said that American merchant ships have always been very important, but recently their value and importance have declined. But today has reached a period of rectification. All countries are now building new-style merchant ships. The American people want the American government to participate in this competition, and want the United States to use its own ships. Therefore, the government's responsibility lies in investigating whether the American merchant ships meet the people's hopes and national needs. Former disguised subsidies, such as mail delivery contracts and shipbuilding loans, have all failed. Therefore, direct subsidies are advocated, based on the difference between the cost of shipbuilding and operations in the United States and other countries, and the amount of many foreign subsidies for shipping operations. As for the number of subsidies, President Roosevelt did not specify, wanting Congress to decide on a number sufficient to offset the above-mentioned difference. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Rice Seeds from Thousands of Years Ago Actually Sprout 45

The Mystery of Life is Truly Inconceivable

Shizuoka News The recent sprouting of rice seeds from thousands of years ago, found inside a statue of Yakushi Nyorai (Medicine Buddha) in Japan, has caused a stir in academic circles. The details are as follows: Zensui Temple in Koka County, Shiga Prefecture, has a statue of Yakushi Nyorai with a tradition of thousands of years. Last year, at the end of the year, a crack suddenly appeared in the chest of the statue. The temple authorities invited a sculptor to repair it. Surprisingly, about one liter of rice seeds was found inside the chest of the statue. When the news spread, scholars across the country were greatly stirred and rushed to take some as research material. At the same time, the authorities of Nakaizumi Agricultural School in Shizuoka Prefecture also obtained twelve of the rice seeds for experiments. As a result, two of them were able to sprout. Japanese academic circles are amazed at the mystery of life, and it is particularly inconceivable that this object was obtained from inside a statue of the Medicine Buddha, whose great vow is to benefit all beings and satisfy their hunger. (World News Agency)

Formation of New Hungarian Cabinet 46

Budapest, Hungarian Capital Gomös has organized a new cabinet today. Regent Horthy has approved the list of the new cabinet. Compared with the previous cabinet, only three seats, finance, commerce, and internal affairs, have been changed. Political observers say that the speed with which Gomös formed the cabinet shows that Count Bethlen and the large landowners' opposition to the proposed election reform plan has suffered a setback. (4th National Press Agency)

Soviet Russia Actively Prepares for War in Outer Mongolia 76

Kulun Town as the Center for Military Operations

And Constructing a Second Line of Defense

Harbin Dispatch from the *North China Daily News*, February 22nd: A certain foreigner recently traveled in Mongolia and has now returned from Kulun to this place. He described the situation in Outer Mongolia, saying that the entire Outer Mongolia is currently preparing for war. This reveals the plan that Soviet Russia is currently implementing. Soviet Russia has recently begun to rapidly consolidate the defense of the entire Outer Mongolia. In the past, transportation relied entirely on camels, but now it is almost entirely replaced by automobiles. The vehicles are mostly loaded with military supplies. At the same time, all major roads and branch roads have been repaired and completed. The main road from Zhangjiakou to Kulun is particularly well-maintained. All places requiring bridges have been built, and the road surface is paved with stones, making it extremely strong. Heavy-duty vehicles can travel unimpeded. In the past, this road required constant repairs, but now it is passable year-round. Three gas stations have been built along the way to provide fuel for vehicles. One station even has a workshop and vehicle depot, storing many vehicles that can be deployed at any time, and is equipped with a wireless telegraph office. An airfield has also been built along the road for airplanes to land. At the stopping stations along the road, there are about fifty guards stationed. Kulun Town has become the center for military operations. From a general observation, Kulun already belongs to a border defense area. Everywhere one looks, one sees robust soldiers, with very few people in civilian clothes. About sixty kilometers away from Kulun, there is a complete arsenal connected by a first-class asphalt road. The factory produces a large number of bullets every day, and there is a workshop for repairing various weapons. All the personnel in the arsenal are engineers, gun experts, and skilled workers selected from major Soviet arsenals. The factory is equipped with wireless electricity. Four kilometers away from the arsenal, there is a small town where various troops are stationed. It is not known what kind of military supplies are stored in the town because ordinary people are not allowed to enter. On the other side of Kulun, about nine kilometers away from the town, there are two airfields, one for commercial use and one larger one specifically for military use. The airfield has aircraft storage, workshops, power plants, a wireless station, and barracks for staff and workers. Although Kulun is far from the border between China and Manchuria, one thing is strange: the residents of the town do not have a spirit of excitement, but are all fearful as if a great disaster is about to befall them. This is probably due to the fact that a part of the residents strongly hate Russia. The Russian-language *Harbin Daily* once published an article discussing the current situation in Mongolia, saying that the Soviet secret police are now making every effort to eliminate anti-Russian elements, either by deporting them, arresting them, or even executing those who do not support the Soviet system. Many lamas and Mongolians in Outer Mongolia have recently moved to the area bordering Inner Mongolia and Outer Mongolia. The road from Kulun to Doron Nor is one of the important roads for Mongolia, and now commercial traffic is prohibited and is used exclusively for military purposes and is very well maintained. Heavy-duty trucks carrying cement buckets are constantly driving in that direction. The authorities prohibit ordinary people from approaching the road, so it is impossible to know the specifics. Large quantities of military supplies, such as rifles, machine guns, and bullets, are transported along the road every day, and there are military escorts, sometimes accompanied by armored vehicles. Outer Mongolia has no defenses to rely on in the event of war, so Soviet Russia has built a strong line of defense in the Irkutsk province along the Transbaikal border, like a continuous chain. This is clearly to prepare a second line of defense in case the first line of defense is lost. From all these circumstances, it is sufficient to show that Soviet Russia is sparing no effort to consolidate border defenses and prepare for war.

Page 8

Opening of the Hubei Provincial Administrative Conference 77

Zhang Qun's Opening Speech Outlines Four Meanings

With Production and Construction as Central Issues

Hankou Correspondence: In order to reform the district office system in Hubei Province, universally carry out land declarations, select central construction work, determine methods for people to perform labor service, and implement the group management district system, the provincial government specifically convened a province-wide administrative conference on the first of this month. However, because the commissioners of each district were either far from the province or unable to arrive in time, it was changed to the fourth. At 9:00 a.m. that day, an enlarged party and government memorial week was first held in the provincial government, followed by the opening ceremony of the province-wide administrative conference. Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun, Civil Affairs Director Meng Guangpeng, Finance Director Jia Shiyi, Construction Director Li Fanyi, Education Director Cheng Qibao, Committee Members Lu Zhu, Fan Xiji, Wu Guozhen, Li Shucheng, and administrative commissioners of each district, Yu Dianshu, Li Huiwu, Liu Fu, Cheng Ruhai, Yang Enxi, Shi Yuling, Lei Xiaocen, Cheng Zerun, Luo Jingyou, etc., all attended. Zhang Xueliang, director of the Generalissimo's Headquarters, also attended. After Chairman Zhang Qun announced the opening of the conference, Zhang Xueliang delivered a speech. After the speech, the first general assembly was held. Zhang Qun delivered the opening speech, which stated: "Last year in March, senior administrative personnel from various provinces were summoned by Chairman Chiang to Nanchang for training. Before going to Nanchang, the commissioners of our province first gathered at the provincial government twice, discussing in detail matters that should be promoted and reformed in the localities. Although there has been considerable progress in governance over the past year, after examining the past and looking to the future, there are still things that have not been fully realized as expected and still need to be promoted. In the past year, matters such as the joint office of the provincial government, the abolition of bureaus and the establishment of sections in the county government, the improvement of the security team system, the unified collection and expenditure of security funds, and the implementation of the four major political agendas have all been major reforms in past governance. Now, according to orders, reforming the district office system, universally carrying out land declarations, selecting central construction work, determining methods for people to perform labor service, and implementing the regulations on group management districts are all important policies that need to be implemented urgently in the future. All of the above can be listed as three major issues. First, the issue of system reform. In terms of the administrative system, the reorganization of counties and districts is consistent, eliminating the long-standing malpractices of separation between superiors and subordinates, perfunctory compliance, and following old ways. In terms of the security system, there must be repeated training and repeated retirement, from a small-scale conscription system to a large-scale conscription system. Second, the issue of production and construction. Matters such as people performing labor service, selecting central construction work, and conscripting labor for construction, developing local production and land, must be designed and implemented to make them effective. Third, the issue of land consolidation. Matters such as land surveys and declarations must be implemented properly with reference to local conditions. All of these matters require gathering collective wisdom and jointly planning for implementation. This is the main purpose of convening the province-wide administrative conference. The above-mentioned issues actually contain four meanings: first, governance methods; second, governance personnel; third, cultivating the strength of the people; and fourth, utilizing land. The purpose of governance methods is how to promote laws and regulations. The purpose of governing people is to study how to be a person, how to use people, and how to be employed by people. The purpose of cultivating the strength of the people is to create new people suitable for the modern era, striving to make people make the best use of their talents. The purpose of utilizing land is to create fertile land rich in production, striving to make the land make the best use of its advantages. The above four meanings, whether they belong to the governing aspect of governance methods and governance personnel, or to the political aspect of the people and land, are all principles that should be paid attention to in the province's politics, and also the basis for discussion in this conference. Recently, the international situation is changing, and the military suppression of bandits is progressing. We who bear the responsibility of politics should take advantage of this opportunity to quickly make plans for revitalization. Chairman Chiang once quoted Guanzi's saying 'Teach the people strength through death, teach the people wealth through labor' to instruct us. Although the two sentences are simple, they are actually the most refined in our country's political philosophy, and also the most essential in today's political facilities. Only when we want to teach the people through labor, we must devote ourselves to the utmost. Only when we want to teach the people through death, we must not stop until death. This is what I hope to share with my colleagues." Then, the list of review committee members was announced. The first group was civil administration, convened by Meng Guangpeng; the second group was finance, convened by Jia Shiyi; the third group was education, convened by Cheng Qibao; the fourth group was construction and water conservancy, convened by Li Fanyi; and the fifth group was security, convened by Fan Xiji. On that day, five proposals were discussed: (1) Proposed by the chairman, a draft of detailed rules for the implementation of the method of establishing district offices in various counties; (2) Proposed by the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments, a plan for implementing district offices in various counties and formulating methods for raising funds for district offices; (3) Proposed by the Fourth District Commissioner, whether the qualifications of incumbent district chiefs and district members can be appropriately relaxed when establishing district offices; (4) Proposed by the Sixth District Commissioner, how to raise funds for the re-surveying of Baojia households and the reorganization of various land tax registers in each county after the establishment of district offices; (5) Proposed by the Eleventh District Commissioner, to move the district offices of the first district attached to the county seat to other more important cities and towns to avoid being equal to superfluous branches. It was decided to submit the cases to the first and second groups for combined review. At this point, the meeting was adjourned. In the afternoon, the first and second groups held a review meeting, completed the review of the above five cases, signed their opinions, and prepared to submit them to the second general assembly for approval and implementation. The meeting period was tentatively set for five days. Each general assembly invited a party, government, or military leader to attend and provide guidance. In addition to Zhang Xueliang's guidance at the first general assembly on the first day to discuss civil administration cases, He Chengjun, director of the Pacification Headquarters, was invited to guide the discussion of financial reorganization cases at the second general assembly on the fifth. Ai Yuying, Wang Shaoyou, and Liu Minggao, standing committee members of the provincial party department, were invited to guide the discussion of production and construction cases at the third general assembly on the sixth. Wen Qun, director of the Generalissimo's Headquarters, was invited to guide the discussion of rural education cases at the fourth general assembly on the seventh. Shi Yancheng, president of the High Court, was invited to guide the discussion of security team reorganization cases at the fifth general assembly on the eighth. In the afternoon of that day, the general assembly was closed. (4th)

Jiangxi Provincial Chamber of Commerce Delegates Conference 78

More Than One Hundred Delegates from Seventy-Three Chambers of Commerce Attend

Each Delegate Reports on the Decline of Commerce

Nanchang Correspondence: The united organization of the Jiangxi provincial business community existed before the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, called the Office. After the seventeenth year, it was changed to the Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce. However, since then, bandit disasters have spread, traffic has been blocked, and many counties and towns have been occupied by bandits. Therefore, in the past seven years, the two convocations of the full delegates conference have not reached the legal quorum. Now that the bandits have been pacified, a provincial chamber of commerce conference was specifically held on the second. A total of 93 county and town chambers of commerce were selected as delegates. More than 100 delegates from 73 chambers of commerce attended. Representatives from the Pacification Headquarters, the provincial and municipal party departments, the provincial and municipal governments, the Nanchang Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and other organizations and groups all participated in the opening ceremony. The venue was set up at the Wanshou Palace Municipal Chamber of Commerce. At 10:00 a.m., the opening ceremony was held. Wang Jianwu, standing committee member of the Nanchang Municipal Chamber of Commerce, presided. After performing the ceremony, he reported on the reorganization of the Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce, stating that since the reorganization of the Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce in the seventeenth year, due to bandit disasters, most local chambers of commerce were dissolved in name only, and no one was responsible. Last year, the provincial party department and the provincial government felt that it was necessary to urgently organize a united association of chambers of commerce in the province, so they appointed Wang Mingxuan and others as reorganization committee members. There were originally 155 chambers of commerce in various counties and towns. Because chambers of commerce in Dexing Yunmenling and other places did not have representatives attending, there were only 113 chambers of commerce. 93 chambers of commerce elected representatives, more than two-thirds. As of now, 73 chambers of commerce have reported their attendance, with 123 representatives. After the chairman's report, representatives from Yujiang, Wanzai, Yihuang, Jishui, Futian, Xinyu, Dayu, Yichun, and other places reported on the impact of the decline of local specialties on commerce. Then, representatives from the Pacification Headquarters and the provincial party department delivered speeches. Wang Jianwu gave a reply on behalf of the presidium. The ceremony was completed at 12:00 and the meeting was adjourned.

Many proposals were sent by chambers of commerce in various counties and cities, roughly divided into (1) 8 cases of blockade, (2) 3 cases of financial relief, (3) 1 case of textiles, (4) 1 case of the chamber of commerce's own organization, (5) 7 cases of industrial and commercial development, (6) 7 cases of transportation business, (7) 2 cases of commercial self-defense, (8) 7 cases of disaster relief, (9) 1 case of tungsten ore relief, (10) 2 cases of store rent, (11) 3 cases of commercial request for exemption from military service, (12) 9 cases of military service allocation borrowing and advance payment, (13) 11 cases of business tax, (14) 13 cases of post-bandit area donation, (15) 12 cases of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, (16) more than 10 other cases, and there are still cases regarding the improvement of local products in various places in order to develop commerce, but they have not been compiled. The conference is scheduled to begin discussing each proposal and elect committee members on the fourth. After the closing of the meeting, they will visit various experimental areas. (March 3rd)

Guangdong Provincial Finance Department Investigates Taxes in Various Regions 79

Organizing Investigation Teams to Go to Various Counties

Shantou Correspondence: The number of taxes in Guangdong Province is as numerous as the hairs of an ox, and it is impossible to count them all. Even the Finance Department feels that it does not know the total number. Therefore, the department has an organization of tax investigation teams, which go to various counties to investigate. From last year to the present, the investigation has not yet been completed. The head of the investigation team, Zhang Zimo, recently arrived in Shantou from the province on the Haiheng wheel. The members of his team are Feng Guangren, Lin Shaohan, Yao Shijin, Chen Chengtian, Liao Xiang, etc. Zhang Zimo said that the areas to be investigated this time are Shantou, Chaoan, Jieyang, Puning, Chaoyang, Chenghai, Raoping, and Nanao. The investigation matters can be divided into seven points: (1) The types and actual amounts of income of the county and city governments and their affiliated agencies, groups, and district and township offices; (2) The types, actual amounts, and uses of expenditures of county agencies and local groups; (3) All items of taxes and donations collected or paid in each county, city, district, and township, including the name, tax rate, use, actual amount of income, collecting agency, whether it has been submitted to the competent authority for approval, entrusted or contracted, or public bidding, and the people's ability to bear the tax; (4) The names, tax rates, collection methods, uses, and annual total amounts of taxes and fees collected by people's organizations in various counties and cities, such as party departments at all levels, councils, education associations, chambers of commerce, labor unions, schools at all levels, hospitals, charitable halls, orphanages, and other charitable organizations, and which agency approved them; (5) Situation of receiving fees; (6) People's economic situation and ability to bear; (7) Whether the agencies and companies entrusted or contracted by the national and provincial taxes and the municipal and county governments to collect taxes are harsh and the situation. The above seven items are the outline of the investigation given by Zhang Zimo. However, it is impossible to predict the results of the investigation, because the number of taxes in Chaozhou and Meizhou is countless. There are things that are taxed more than ten times, and there are things that must pay donations when passing through the border. There are also donations for conscripts, women's marriage donations, dowry donations, temple wish donations, vegetarian donations, vegetarian donations, repentance donations, paper money donations, incense candle donations, superstition donations, and lamp oil donations. The names are established separately, and taxes are everywhere, so the people are all groaning under the weak government.

Guangdong Province Issues Short-Term Treasury Bills 80

Total Amount is Four Million Yuan

Guangzhou Correspondence: Recently, in order to reorganize finance, the Guangdong Provincial Finance Department issued four million yuan of short-term financial treasury bills for the 24th year of the Republic of China, with a monthly interest rate of one percent, guaranteed by the province's business tax. The issuance is scheduled to begin on March 11. After the issuance, the principal and interest will be repaid in equal installments over four months, starting from the end of the second month. The treasury bills are divided into three types: ten yuan, fifty yuan, and one hundred yuan, totaling 200,000 ten-yuan bills, 30,000 fifty-yuan bills, and 5,000 fifty-yuan bills. The issuance regulations have been discussed and approved by the provincial affairs meeting on February 26 and are recorded as follows:

Article 1: The Guangdong Provincial Government issues short-term treasury bills for the purpose of reorganizing finance, named the Guangdong Province Short-Term Financial Treasury Bills for the 24th year of the Republic of China. Article 2: The total amount of the treasury bills is set at four million yuan. Article 3: The treasury bills are guaranteed by the provincial treasury's revenue from the province's business tax and deed tax. From the date of issuance, the issuance period is one month. After the issuance, the principal and interest will be repaid in equal installments over four months, starting from the end of the second month. The order will be determined by drawing lots. The dates for drawing lots are set on the last day of the second month, the third month, the fourth month, and the fifth month to repay the principal and interest. It is stipulated that silver dollars will be used for payment. Those who want to take Guangdong Provincial Bank's convertible notes are also allowed. Article 4: The interest rate of the treasury bills is a monthly interest rate of one percent, calculated monthly according to the order of drawing lots. That is, for the first month's drawing, one yuan of interest is given for every hundred yuan. For the second month, two yuan of interest is given for every hundred yuan, and so on. Article 5: After the treasury bills are issued, from the end of the second month to the end of the fifth month, the Finance Department will allocate the amount of principal and interest due for the month from the revenue of business tax and deed tax and hand it over to the paper money supervision committee of the Provincial Bank for safekeeping, so that it can be allocated to the Guangdong Provincial Bank after the drawing of lots for the repayment of principal and interest. Article 6: The issuance, promotion, and repayment of principal and interest of the treasury bills shall be handled by the Finance Department entrusted to the Guangdong Provincial Bank. Commercial banks and silver shops in Guangzhou City, as well as miscellaneous shops, may receive and promote the bills in accordance with the provisions of Article 10 of these regulations. Article 7: The treasury bills are divided into three types: one hundred yuan, fifty yuan, and ten yuan. Article 8: The treasury bills are in bearer form. Article 9: The treasury bills are scheduled to be issued on March 11, 24th year of the Republic of China. Article 10: The Guangdong Provincial Bank issues the treasury bills at a 7% discount on the face value. Dealers receive the bills at 93 yuan of provincial convertible notes per 100 yuan of face value. Of the 7 yuan discount, 2 yuan is stipulated as the dealer's commission, and the remaining 5 yuan goes to the bill purchaser, which means that the bill purchaser purchases the bill from the dealer at a 5% discount on the face value. Article 11: Bill purchasers or dealers may freely mortgage, buy, and sell the treasury bills from the date of issuance to the end of the fifth month, and may also mortgage them to the Guangdong Provincial Bank and use them as security deposits for banks, as well as security deposits or guarantees for other official duties. Article 12: Anyone who forges the treasury bills or damages credit will be punished according to law. Article 13: These regulations shall come into effect from the date of promulgation. (February 28th)

Fuzhou Commerce Can Be Expected to Turn Around 81

Local Products from Northern Fujian Will Be Transported to the Province in Large Quantities for Market

Fuzhou Correspondence: There are two commercial ports in Fujian: Xiamen in southern Fujian and Fuzhou in northern Fujian. Because the four items of wood, tea, paper, and bamboo shoots produced in northern Fujian are all exported through Fuzhou and transferred to domestic and foreign countries, and most of the foreign goods, seafood, silk, and fabrics imported by Fuzhou are also sold in northern Fujian. In recent years, due to the disturbance of the Red Bandits in northern Fujian, the local area was in chaos, people fled, and the production of various products was completely cut off. The purchasing power of the people was also greatly reduced. Fuzhou's commerce was affected by this and fell into extreme decline. The wood, tea, paper, and bamboo shoot firms could not make any profit and stopped business one after another. The silk and fabric shops were unable to bear the losses and went bankrupt, resulting in one-third of the loans issued by money shops being unrecoverable, with no hope of principal or interest. The money shops then uniformly withdrew the bills and stopped issuing notes, and the business community became even more stagnant due to tight credit. The precarious situation seemed to be unsustainable. Fortunately, since the summer of last year, the Red Bandits in northern Fujian have been defeated by the National Army, and various counties have been recovered one after another. The refugees who fled to other places were sent back to their hometowns in batches by the government. On the one hand, the rural financial relief office set up in the province organized cooperative societies in the villages and towns of the bandit-affected counties and lent money to farmers, allowing them to engage in planting and farming. After half a year of pacification, local order has gradually stabilized, and the rural economy has also become slightly active. Therefore, since the winter of last year, cloth, oil, and other goods transported from Fuzhou to northern Fujian have gradually become popular. Since the beginning of this year, the amount of paper and bamboo shoots transported from northern Fujian to Fuzhou has also increased. Now, in order to resume business, the tea and wood firms have decided to send partners to the mountains of northern Fujian with money to place orders, so that they can be transported to the province in large quantities for the market in the late spring and early summer. However, this capital must be borrowed from the money shops to be active. Therefore, the Minhou County Chamber of Commerce advised the money shops to uniformly open the market on the twelfth day of the second lunar month, the birthday of the Earth God, and issue notes and lend money as usual, so that commerce can circulate and business can develop. Therefore, it is expected that the Fuzhou business community can be expected to turn around this year. However, Wang Meihui, a prominent merchant in the city and standing committee member of the county chamber of commerce, who opened Tongcheng Porcelain Shop, Hengji Customs Brokerage, and Chang'an Shipping Company (i.e., Chang'an Steamer), suddenly went aground recently, owing a debt of 1.3 million yuan, which caused a great shock to the business community. The reason for this is that Wang has been operating flour in Shanghai for the past two years, losing more than one million yuan, which led to poor turnover. Among them, the Henghe Money Shop opened by Luo Mianhou, chairman of the county chamber of commerce committee, was owed the most, about 300,000 yuan. Now Luo and others are coming out to maintain it, so that it can continue to operate to avoid affecting the market. In addition, the price of rice has risen from 8 yuan to 12 yuan per stone in less than a month because the customs levies full tax on the import of foreign rice, and grain merchants take the opportunity to manipulate prices, which has greatly affected people's food. The Chamber of Commerce is also scheduled to hold a meeting today (2nd) to discuss restrictions. The first step is to prevent further increases, and then persuade rice merchants to expand their sources to match supply and demand for mediation. (March 2nd)

The New Regulations on House Tax in Jiangsu Province and the Appeal of the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce 82

Farmers and Businesses Are Struggling, and Local Areas Can Hardly Bear Additional Burdens

House Taxes in Various Counties Should Remain as They Were

Wuxi Dispatch: The Jiangsu Provincial Government has decided to implement the collection of house tax from residents starting March 1st, and to increase the tax on storefront properties to 15%. Orders have been issued to various counties to actively implement this. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce believes that these new house tax regulations have not gone through legal procedures and violate the Central Government's resolutions. Yesterday, they sent telegrams to various ministries and departments of the Central Government, as well as the Jiangsu Provincial Government's Departments of Civil Affairs and Finance, and the Jiangsu Provincial Tax Supervision Committee, requesting a halt to the implementation. The original telegram is recorded below:

"The house tax in Jiangsu Province originated in the late Qing Dynasty and was originally a revenue-generating measure. Therefore, it was based on a percentage of the rent. Wuxi currently collects 10% of the monthly rent, but only on storefronts and not on residential properties. This is because housing is essential for people's lives. Residential properties are different from storefronts, and the interior of the country is different from metropolitan areas. Where supply exceeds demand, more revenue can be generated. According to Dr. Sun Yat-sen’s Outline of National Reconstruction, the government should work with the people to plan and build various types of houses for the people's residence. How can people's housing be subjected to extortion? This is not in line with the Party and the State's emphasis on people's livelihood. However, we recently saw reports stating that Jiangsu Province has passed regulations on house taxes for all counties, regardless of whether the houses are self-owned or rented, storefronts or residences, in both urban and rural areas. Rented houses will be taxed at 8% of the monthly rent, storefronts at 15%. Self-owned houses will be taxed at 0.8 per thousand of the assessed value for residences and 1.5 per thousand for storefronts. It is also stipulated that this will be implemented immediately. Taxing residential properties will inevitably cause disturbance, and increasing the tax on storefronts by half is clearly an increase in burden.

We respectfully note that the Central Government convened the Second National Financial Conference in May of last year, deeply aware of the deteriorating social economy, the inability of farmers to support themselves, and the increasing decline of industry and commerce. Therefore, the abolition of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies was listed as an important agenda item. In his instructions, Premier Wang Jingwei of the Executive Yuan repeatedly emphasized the severe impoverishment of rural areas, the extreme poverty of society, and the need for relief for the people. He said that he could not bear to levy taxes and extract the people's lifeblood, and almost shed tears. Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi stated in his opening remarks that there were many tasks in planning for recovery, and that the urgency and importance should be carefully considered. Regarding local defense, transportation, education and other policies, he said that efforts should be made to utilize the capabilities of self-governance and self-defense to reduce expenditure and tax burdens. The conference passed a resolution to establish tax supervision committees in all provinces and cities to oversee the abolition of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, and issued a declaration, solemnly stating that in the future, any items of income that involve heavy burdens and disturbances to the people must be eliminated and rectified. If the excess can be removed first, the people's strength can be given a small respite. Any items of expenditure that are useless or not urgent must be abolished or delayed, and any that are excessive or wasteful must be reduced. Being able to reduce expenditure is no different from creating new sources of revenue, and being able to reduce fees eliminates the need to increase taxes. His words were profound and clear, showing the government's concern for the people's suffering and its great determination to abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies. The local people were moved to tears.

Less than a year has passed, and the people are longing for timely rain, but Jiangsu Province is instead enacting new regulations to collect house tax, increasing the tax on storefronts by half and extending it to residential properties. Is this in line with the Central Government's efforts to abolish exorbitant taxes and reduce the people's burden? According to Article 3 of the Provisional Measures for Central Government Supervision of Local Finance, when provinces and municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan need to change tax items, increase or decrease tax rates, or raise public debt, they should, in accordance with the law, formulate a plan and submit it to the Ministry of Finance for review and signature, and then submit it to the Executive Yuan to be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and resolution, and then submit it to the National Government for approval. Article 4 states that counties and cities may not change tax items without legal basis. When there is a need to increase or decrease tax rates, or raise public debt, they should, in accordance with the law, formulate a plan and, before the establishment of the county and city councils, convene local legal entities for open discussion, and submit it to the Finance Department for review and signature, and then submit it to the Provincial Government for deliberation and approval, and then submit it to the Ministry of Finance for record. Article 7 states that local governments at all levels may not implement any changes to tax items, increases or decreases in tax rates, or raising public debt without approval in accordance with the provisions of Articles 3 and 4 of this law, and may not include them in the budget. The regulations are very clear and strict. Now that the house tax in Jiangsu Province is for the expenses of various counties, even if the local areas really need to increase or decrease it, it seems that they should, in accordance with the law, listen to open discussions in the various counties. It is not appropriate to make a decision directly in the province, and before going through legal procedures, it should not be implemented in the province or the counties. This is clearly stipulated by law and should be strictly observed by officials and the people.

At a time when farmers and businesses are struggling and local areas can hardly bear additional burdens, the house tax in Jiangsu Province should remain as it was and should not be changed lightly, lest it cause more disturbances. If it is for the purpose of improving public security, officials and the people must work together. The Baojia system is currently being implemented, and various counties are actively promoting it. If it can gradually achieve results, it can reduce the need for security guards. Only by referring to the views of Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi at the Second National Financial Conference, utilizing the capabilities of self-governance and self-defense to reduce expenditure and tax burdens, and by the tax supervision committees of the various provinces and cities fulfilling their responsibilities to report illegal taxes in accordance with the powers conferred by the Central Government, can the problem be solved. This matter concerns changing taxes and increasing the burden on the people. As a local organization, our Chamber is well aware of the people's difficulties. We dare not speak lightly, but we cannot bear not to speak out. Therefore, we dare not avoid severe punishment, and offer our earnest and direct opinions. We respectfully ask for your consideration and acceptance, and request that you immediately halt the implementation and order that the previous regulations be reinstated to avoid disturbances and uphold the rule of law. We await your orders with utmost eagerness. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce kowtows."

Songjiang 83

Conclusion of the Debate on the Daytime Robbery Case

Last winter, when the county launched its winter defense campaign, the Rifeng Gold Store on Fengle Bridge inside the West Gate was suddenly robbed at 9 a.m. Gold bracelets were stolen and the deputy manager, Zhao Houzhuang, was shot and injured. The two robbers escaped over the city wall with the stolen goods. The local military and police authorities considered the daytime robbery to be extremely serious and launched a search and arrest operation. A robber named Zhao Zhiyi was apprehended in Chedun, and a handgun with the markings of the Shanghai Municipal Police Department was found. He was escorted to the county government for interrogation. According to Zhao Zhiyi's confession, he was instigated by bad friends to borrow money and was invited to commit the crime. He stole a gun from his father (who was a detective in the Shanghai Municipal Police Department) and came to Songjiang with his friend, staying at the Songhui Hotel. After obtaining the stolen goods, he handed them over to his bad friend, who fled with them, etc. Later, the county government telegraphed the province for instructions, and he was ordered to be handed over to the local court for investigation and prosecution in accordance with the law. After an investigation by the Prosecutor's Office, a public prosecution was filed. Judge Zhang of the Criminal Court held a trial today (5th), and the witness Zhao Houzhuang testified in court. Zhao Zhiyi's testimony was largely the same as before, but he suddenly changed his story regarding cutting the telephone line. The defendant hired lawyer Gu Shouyi to defend him in court. The judge declared the debate closed and scheduled a date for sentencing.

Wuxi 84

Completion of Aerial Survey

The aerial survey of Wuxi, which began in November of last year, has now been completed after three months. The total area of the county is 1,333 square kilometers, equivalent to 200,000 mu. The accuracy is very reliable. The total cost was 112,273.40 yuan, which has been reported to the provincial government. The reason why it was able to be completed so quickly in a short period of time is that it was time-saving and economical, and the accuracy is more reliable than manual surveying.

Tragic Scene of a Burnt Slum

The area near the Xicheng Road intersection in the county is where many Jiangbei immigrants gather, so the thatched huts are closely packed together, like a beehive. Yesterday (5th) morning at about 3 o'clock, a fire accidentally broke out in the house of Yao Fushun. The flames quickly spread and became uncontrollable, spreading to neighboring huts. The fire brigades of various sections heard the alarm and immediately rushed to the scene with water pumps, doing their best to put out the fire. As a result, 36 thatched huts were burned down. When the fire was raging, the wife of Wu Fugen, Zhou, who lived in a neighboring hut, was burned on her right hand because she was slow to escape. The cries of men, women, and children were unbearable to hear.

Bureau Chief and Staff Dismissed and Investigated

The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Opium Committee previously received a secret report stating that Zhang Yu, the chief of the First Branch Bureau of Wuxi, and Fan Shouchi, a staff member, were involved in bribery in the case of the wanted large opium dealer Wang Guiqing. Therefore, on the 12th of last month, they sent investigator Li Gongfu to Wuxi to thoroughly investigate. However, after Li arrived at the First Branch Bureau, Zhang Yu and Fan Shouchi openly insulted the Provincial Committee. After Chen, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, learned of this, he recorded a demerit against Zhang and Fan for being rash in handling the matter. Yesterday, the county government received an order from the Department of Civil Affairs, stating that Zhang Yu, the chief of the Public Security Branch Bureau of the county, and Fan Shouchi, a staff member, had openly insulted the Provincial Committee and were extremely absurd. They were immediately dismissed from their posts and investigated in connection with the case. The vacant positions were to be filled by other committee members. It is said that because Magistrate Yan went to Shanghai to negotiate fundraising matters and had not yet returned to Wuxi, and Chief Chen Yuchu of the Public Security Bureau was also attending a public security conference in the provincial government, the successors to the positions in the Public Security Bureau have not yet been decided.

Changshu 85

Investigation and Prohibition of Blasting to Quarry Stone

The roadbeds of the Suchang and Xichang highways have been completed, and bidding is now being invited to pave the macadam road surface. Unexpectedly, the contractors, greedy for petty profits, are quarrying stone at the foot of Xishan in the county, using a large amount of explosives every day to blast and chisel the stone. However, the area is a scenic area, with historical sites and tombs everywhere, many of which have been damaged. Local citizens have petitioned the county authorities to investigate and prohibit this. Recently, more than 300 people from other provinces have arrived in the Xiangxiang area of Xishan, bringing a large number of tools and gunpowder, preparing to extract a large amount of stone. The Public Security Bureau, upon hearing this, believes that privately quarrying stone is a violation of the prohibition regulations and has sent police to stop them.

Changzhou 86

Gangsters Send Threatening Letters to Villagers

The Yinsha area of Weicun in the northern Wu Yi township has always been a place where bandits appear. Last year, Liu Xingsu, a wealthy resident of the city, went to the countryside to collect rent in Yinsha and was kidnapped by bandits. His whereabouts are still unknown. Unexpectedly, Xu Xirong, a farmer in Qingshui Gou near Weicun, found a red letter on the ground when his daughter was opening the door the day before yesterday. She picked it up and told her father, Xirong, who, after opening it, realized that it was a threatening letter from gangsters. The letter demanded that a large sum of money be raised quickly and sent to the Dragon Emperor Temple for negotiation within three days. If the deadline was missed, they would gather their men and burn and kill the entire family. Xirong is now extremely uneasy, and the nearby residents are also panicked.

Zhenjiang 87

Completion of the Beigushan Meteorological Station

Since its expansion, the Jiangsu Provincial Meteorological Station has found that the original location and buildings were insufficient for its needs. A meteorological station was built on the central peak of Beigushan. Construction has been underway for several months, and the project has now been completed. The interior layout, such as the installation of instruments and the arrangement of miscellaneous items, has been completed. They are now engaged in organizing documents and will be able to move into the new station and begin working within days.

Most County Warehouses Completed

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance previously ordered all counties to actively complete the construction of county warehouses. According to the survey, more than 40 counties, including Taixian and Dongtai, have been established and are ready for use. In January of this year, three new warehouses were built in Jurong, four in Wujin, two in Taixian, one in Shuyang, three additional warehouses were set up in Yixing, two each in Jintan and Rugao, and one each in Songjiang, Taixing, and Jiangdu. Seven of the ten provincial agricultural warehouses have now been completed. Only Suqian, Huaian, and Rugao are still under construction. In addition, the Department of Finance also plans to build three or four provincial warehouses in Jurong and other counties.

Yixing 88

County Magistrate Zhong Accused of Torture

Zhong Jingcheng, the county magistrate of Yixing, recently brought relatives of Gu Tongsun, who embezzled land tax and escaped from the detention center, to the county and interrogated them late at night, torturing them to find out Gu's whereabouts. The family members of the injured Chu Shao have now filed a complaint with the Chief Prosecutor of the Jiangsu High Court, who has approved the dispatch of the Chief Prosecutor of the Wuxi Local Branch Court to Yixing to investigate the case.

Nantong 89

Strike at Guanyinshan Town

Feng Guangying, a villager from Guanyinshan Town east of the city who sells cloth, saw a red paper package on the road and picked it up out of greed. Two wandering soldiers, Li Xueqian and Li Yusheng, searched the villager and found that the package contained bullets. They accused him of being a bandit and tied him up to take him to the city. At the same time, the stationed troops arrived and mistakenly fired shots, arousing public anger. The entire town went on strike. After the incident, the local people sent the two wandering soldiers and the villager who picked up the package to the county government.

Haimen 90

Robbery and Assault Near the County Seat

The family of Yu Gu, a farmer near the Old People's Hall west of the county seat, was well-off and was targeted by bandits. Yesterday (2nd) at about 9 p.m., more than ten bandits suddenly came, speaking in a local accent, each carrying wooden sticks. They broke into the house, first grabbed Yu Gu, forced him to hand over silver dollars, and then beat him violently, causing serious injuries to his chest and arms. The bandits then ransacked the house, searching extensively for about an hour before leaving with a shout. After checking, more than ten bolts of cloth and silver ornaments worth about 200 yuan were robbed. Today (3rd), the victim reported the incident to the county government for investigation.

Bust of Smuggling Ring

Wu Ying and Yu Zutang, investigators from the Provincial Anti-Opium Committee, came to Haimen under orders to assist in the anti-opium policy. They have cracked many opium cases in recent days. Yesterday (3rd) afternoon, they learned that Zhang Degong, a native of Shi Jia Town in District One, had established a smuggling ring. They led the police to investigate and seized 29 packages of opium and more than ten sets of opium paraphernalia. Zhang had escaped, but his concubine, Widow Huang, was arrested. They also found fourteen red pill tubes in the home of Wang Chen (the wife of Wang, the patrol chief of the town's water police). Widow Huang, Wang Chen, and the stolen goods were all sent to the county government for interrogation.

Yangzhou 91

Provincial Order to Implement Work Relief in the Eighth and Ninth Districts

The Jiangsu Provincial Department ordered the Jiangdu County Government to instruct the work relief dredging project in the eighth and ninth districts to be implemented as soon as possible during the slack farming season in the spring, after determining the river channels to be dredged, in order to benefit the disaster-stricken farmers. Yesterday (3rd), Magistrate Ma, in order to ensure substantial and widespread benefits, ordered the heads of the Second Section, Tang Jianzhong, and the rice section of the Construction Bureau to go to the eighth and ninth districts to conduct on-site surveys based on the previously determined plan, in order to determine the budget and convene a work relief meeting to approve the construction sequence and dates, so that no township would be neglected. The section chiefs and others departed from Yangzhou yesterday (4th) to inspect Huaizibao first.

Jiaxing 92

Preparation to Establish a Youth Labor Service Corps

Wang Chunong, director of the Jiaxing County Martial Arts Hall, recognizing the importance of youth labor service, initiated the organization of the Jiaxing Youth Labor Service Corps, in order to establish a trend of labor service among the people of the county and eliminate the bad habits of laziness and apathy. Anyone between the ages of twelve and forty can join the corps. Yesterday, the initiators sent letters to young people from all walks of life to support and join.

Shaoxing 93

Provincial Allocation of Large Sums to Dredge Sand Outside the Sanjiang Sluice

Outside the Sanjiang Sluice, a key waterway for water discharge in Shaoxiao, sand has recently accumulated, reaching a length of fifteen li, so that the water stored in the inner river cannot be discharged. The director of the Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau came to Shaoxing to inspect and decided to hire workers to dredge it. The county government submitted a method to the province for approval. It is now reported that the provincial government, considering that the sluice is related to the water conservancy of Shaoxiao County, has decided to allocate 16,000 yuan from the work relief funds for the Water Conservancy Bureau to be responsible for hiring workers to dredge it.

Sheng County 94

Relief Association Borrows Money to Conduct Price Stabilization

The Sheng County Relief Branch Association decided to entrust the Shanghai Jiaxu All Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association to purchase 5,000 dan of duty-free foreign rice for price stabilization in the county, because the disaster situation in the county last year was very serious and the implementation of spring price stabilization was imminent. The committee members of the Relief Association have borrowed 35,000 yuan in silver from the Sheng County Agricultural and Industrial Bank and the Shengxin Local Savings Bank to purchase the rice. The heads of the two banks, Wang Zhengjin, have agreed to lend the money. It is said that when the duty-free foreign rice arrives, it will be about three yuan cheaper per dan than the price in rice stores.

Hangzhou 95

Large Group of Captured Bandits Escorted to Xunyang for Rehabilitation

The Zhejiang Security Column and the Wang Brigade of the Fifth Division previously captured more than 2,000 Red Army officers and soldiers in the Gan-East area and escorted them to Hangzhou for custody. After sending more than 30 important bandit leaders to Gan for interrogation, it was learned that more than 200 of the soldiers were good people from the border areas of various provinces such as Gan, Wan, and Min, who were conscripted by the bandits. After being interrogated and identified, they were released and sent back to their original homes. The remaining 1,792 Red Army soldiers below the rank of platoon leader have been ordered by Chairman Chiang to be escorted to the Xunyang Rehabilitation Institute for rehabilitation. The Security Office specially dispatched a section member, Wei Hanhua, leading a battalion of soldiers, to escort them by special express train with multiple freight cars attached last night to Nanjing for transfer to a ship to Jiujiang.

Mingguang 96

County Government Convenes a Zonal Planning Meeting

The county government, in accordance with the "Organizational Regulations of Zonal Offices" promulgated by the General Headquarters of the Commander-in-Chief, convened a zonal planning meeting yesterday (2nd). As a result, the original five zones were reorganized into three zones. The zonal offices are located in Mingguang, Jiashan, and Zilaiqiao. It will be implemented as soon as it is submitted to the province for approval.

Local News

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association Discuss and Determine Measures to Revitalize the Market 97

Conducted separately by the two groups

Premier Wang Replied by Telegram and Instructed the Ministry and the Municipal Council to Discuss

The Chamber of Commerce Appointed Representatives to Prepare for a Personal Presentation

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, regarding the issue of market relief, since the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Local Association, and the Silver and Money Guilds and other four groups have been working separately, the financial situation has gradually become more flexible and the market has stabilized. Recently, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association, in order to seek further expansion, have each formed specialized committees to study specific methods of revitalization. After several discussions, five measures have been decided upon and will be earnestly implemented. The details are as follows:

Five Specific Measures

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association have formally developed five specific measures to revitalize the market: (1) Bills of exchange from various industries should be discounted by silver and money businesses. If there is proper collateral, the silver and money businesses should accept them. The Central Bank should also provide rediscounting to silver and money businesses. (2) Title deeds and land license certificates should be added as collateral for Central Bank notes. (3) Title deeds and land license certificates should be added as savings collateral. (4) Silver and money businesses should continue to send account books to various stores as usual, but they may determine the amount of overdrafts granted. The stores themselves should also strive to improve their organization. (5) If silver and money businesses mortgage goods or real estate to the Central Bank, the Bank of China, or the Bank of Communications, or discount bills, they should accept them as much as possible. The above five measures have been submitted to the Ministry of Finance by the two groups, and letters have been sent to the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Silver and Money Guilds, requesting compliance.

The Executive Yuan Replies to the Chamber of Commerce

In addition to agreeing on five specific measures with the Local Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce also sent telegrams to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Military Affairs Committee, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and the Ministries of Finance and Industry on March 1, stating the difficulties faced by industry and commerce in Shanghai and requesting that fundamental plans be drawn up quickly. Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a reply from Premier Wang Jingwei of the Executive Yuan, which read: "The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, I have received your telegram. The government has long been considering ways to rescue Shanghai's stagnation. At this time, the world economy is generally tight, and Shanghai, as a major port in the East, can hardly be exempt. In addition, the national crisis is at its height and the countryside is in decline. Tracing the cause of these problems is complex and difficult. The government's policies in recent years have all focused on revitalization as an urgent matter. We cannot limit ourselves to temporary solutions, nor can we shirk our responsibilities. The profitability or loss of Shanghai's commerce is closely related to the prosperity of the entire country. The coordination of information has always been a matter of concern. The section in your telegram concerning the request for relief from twenty industries has been referred to the Ministries of Finance and Industry and the Shanghai Municipal Government for immediate consultation on specific measures, which will be submitted for approval and implementation to provide relief. I hope that your Chamber of Commerce and all sectors will work together to discuss and cope calmly, so that the market can stabilize as soon as possible. I trust that the members of your Chamber of Commerce will understand the importance of cooperation. A special reply, Wang Zhaoming in winter."

Appointed Representatives to Present Personally

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce decided that, although measures to revitalize the market have already been discussed and are being implemented, there is still a need to present them to the government authorities in person. Therefore, at the ninth meeting of the Executive Committee yesterday, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Qin Runqing, and Bei Songsun were appointed as five advisory committee members, and Chairman Yu Zuoting and Supervisory Committee member Du Yuesheng were appointed to visit the government authorities when necessary.

Original Text of the Telegram Reporting the Establishment of the Industrial and Commercial Relief Association 98

Telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek

According to the Guowen News Agency, the text of the telegram sent by the Industrial and Commercial Relief Association to Chairman Chiang yesterday, as reported in the newspaper, was a draft. It has since been modified and sent. The original text is now published as follows: "Respectfully to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Chongqing, We have long admired your achievements in the Party and the State and your concern for the people. All of us in industry and commerce feel love and respect. However, in recent years, we have suffered from internal water and drought famines and external dumping from various countries. In addition, the number of silver exports last year was more than 400 million, and the number of trade deficits was 700 million, leading to economic decline and livelihood difficulties. Moreover, the financial and industrial sectors are still at odds, unable to help each other. Therefore, not only is the countryside on the verge of bankruptcy, but industry and commerce are also in danger. An investigation shows that four out of ten factories in Shanghai have closed down this year, and three out of ten stores have closed down. The number of unemployed workers that can be counted has reached more than 500,000. If we do not take remedial measures immediately, what prospects can we imagine for industry? In view of this, Zhihao and others established the China Industrial and Commercial Relief Association in Shanghai on March 2 this year, with the primary purpose of rescuing industry. In addition to detailing the measures, which will be submitted by telegram for approval, we hereby report by telegram. The entire board of directors of the China Industrial and Commercial Relief Association, the First Special District Citizens' Federation, and the sub-district associations all kowtow."

Observations on the Sharp Drop in Gold Prices in the Financial World 99

Merchants Take the Opportunity to Purchase Foreign Goods at Low Prices

Creating Another Opportunity for Silver Exports

According to the Central News Agency, the gold price situation has been plummeting recently, with new lows being created, reaching a record low of 805 yuan. The market is extremely uncertain. A reporter from the Central News Agency specifically visited a prominent figure in the financial world to ask about the impact of the gold price decline on our society. The figure said that the gold price has fallen from more than 900 yuan to 806 yuan in the past month, a difference of more than 100 yuan. The reason is that countries that use gold want to depress the value of their currency so that their surplus goods can be sold widely in foreign markets. Large domestic accounts are also selling and buying aggressively, resulting in a sharp decline. This phenomenon will naturally have a great impact on our country's industry, commerce, and banks. As foreign currency prices fall, our merchants can take the opportunity to purchase foreign goods at low prices. In other words, this creates another opportunity for silver exports, which is all harmful and no beneficial to China.
