All Primary Schools to Adopt Huanghuagang Revolution Memorial Teaching Materials 167

Central Activities to Be Held Regularly

The Municipal Education Bureau Follows Instructions

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to its affiliated primary schools yesterday, stating: Revolutionary thought and spirit must be cultivated in childhood. The stirring, tragic, and passionate revolutionary events in history should be used to stimulate children's revolutionary emotions and cultivate their revolutionary thought and spirit. In view of this, this bureau has been compiling and selecting supplementary teaching materials for revolutionary memorial days and ordering all schools to adopt them. Now that March 29th is the Huanghuagang Revolution Memorial Day, the supplementary teaching materials for all primary schools should still follow the old plan and be prepared in advance. The following two books are designated as required supplementary teaching materials for all public and private primary schools on the Huanghuagang Revolution Memorial Day: (1) The lower grades should uniformly use the self-compiled edition by this bureau. (2) The middle and upper grades should uniformly use the edition published by the Children's Literature and Art Society. The first type, used by the lower grades, should be purchased by each school from this bureau. The second type, used by the middle and upper grades, should be ordered by each school from the Children's Happiness Society at Jinpanfang near Penglai Road in South Shanghai, or the Children's Morning News Society on Shandong Road, so that each student has a copy to facilitate teaching. As for the prices of the books, the self-compiled edition by this bureau will be sold for 3 silver cents per copy, and the edition published by the Children's Literature and Art Society is originally priced at 2 jiao, but this bureau has negotiated with the publisher to reduce the price by half, with a real price of 1 jiao of silver, in order to reduce the burden on children. In order to improve the teaching effectiveness of all schools, this bureau has also designated that from March 25th to 30th, all primary schools should uniformly hold central activities for the Huanghuagang Revolution Memorial Day. The teaching materials for all subjects and children's activities should be centered on the Huanghuagang Revolution events. In addition to adopting the above designated teaching materials, each school should also formulate detailed plans and implement them conscientiously to achieve significant results. It is hereby ordered that each school comply with the above instructions and report the implementation status to this bureau for review. This is of utmost importance. This order.

Rotary International Conference in the Philippines 170

Chinese Guests Gather in Manila

Gui Shun Gives a Speech, Filipinos Host with Great Hospitality

Guangdong Representatives Dissatisfied with Immigration Law

(Manila Correspondence) During this annual hot carnival season, in order to attract tourists, the 5th Rotary International Conference was also convened in Manila. The representatives of the Xiamen Rotary Club in China were Wang Fuxing, Hong Zhaohuan, Shen Zhizhong, and Ding Xirong. The representatives from Shanghai were Wang Wangting and Mr. and Mrs. Kuang Fuzhuo. Those from Nanjing were Yan Deqing and Mr. and Mrs. Yu Qingsong, and Chen Yuguang (president of Jinling University and president of the Chinese Chemical Society). Lin Fengqi was from Qingdao, Zhu Foling was from Jinan, Mr. and Mrs. Lao Jing'an were from Hangzhou, and Mr. and Mrs. Yang Mianxi and the Luo brothers, Luo Wenhao and Luo Wenjin, were from Hong Kong. They arrived in Manila on the 17th aboard the President Jackson.

Situation: The ship arrived at the dock at 7 o'clock. Representatives of the Philippine Rotary Club (both men and women) and various overseas Chinese community organizations gathered to welcome them. The women wore local costumes, with cicada-wing shirts and floor-length skirts. Their mode of transportation was not modern motorcycles, but the ancient and clumsy horse-drawn carts used to transport goods and people in the Philippine countryside. Their musical instruments were not military music or Westernized elegant music, but bamboo instruments from the primitive era of the Philippines, with a unique antique charm. After leaving the dock, they were taken on a tour of the city before resting briefly at the Manila Hotel. They then took a special express train to Los Baños (two hours by train from Manila) to visit scenic spots. In the evening, they gathered at the Hygiene Lecture Hall. Accommodation was at the discretion of the guests, except for designated locations.

Conference Proceedings: The official opening ceremony was held at 9:30 am on the 18th. The Acting Governor delivered a welcome speech. The Speaker of the Senate delivered a welcome speech on behalf of the Filipino people. The Mayor and the President of the Rotary Club also delivered welcome speeches successively. The Secretary of the Conference then announced the purpose of the conference, followed by singing. The Chairman of the Conference delivered a speech, and representatives from various parties delivered speeches. The conference continued after lunch and adjourned at 5:30 pm. In the evening, the Philippine University Club held a dinner party to welcome the guests. All family members of the Rotary Club representatives were invited to participate. A Philippine women's music team provided entertainment. A lecture was held at 9 o'clock, followed by dancing at 10 o'clock.

On the morning of the 19th, there was singing at 8 am, followed by a conference at 9 am. Representatives delivered speeches successively. There was a photo session at 11:30 am. After lunch, they took a car to visit scenic spots in Marrati (with a radio station). There was a dinner party at 7:30 pm, followed by a variety show.

On the 20th, there was singing at 9 am, followed by a conference at 10 am. There was a dinner party at the Spanish Association at 12 noon, during which speeches were given. A dance party was held at the Manila Hotel in the evening. At 12 midnight, the representatives took the President Coolidge to leave the Philippines.

Summary of Speeches: In his welcome speech on behalf of the Philippine nation, the Speaker of the Philippine Senate explained the importance of holding the Rotary Club conference in Manila, and said that the Filipino people were extremely sincere and hospitable. If foreign guests need food and lodging in the countryside, the Filipino people will sincerely welcome them, which proves that the Filipino people are willing to join hands with foreigners by nature. J. M. Henry, a representative from Guangdong, spoke on the value and significance of organizing tourist groups to foreign countries. He mentioned that narrow nationalism has a negative impact on diplomatic relations, and that the Philippine immigration regulations have a discriminatory attitude towards the import restrictions on overseas Chinese. Most members of the Guangdong Rotary Club were unwilling to come to the Philippines to participate in order not to damage the dignity of the country and individuals. Wang Zhengting and representatives from various countries also delivered routine speeches.

Overseas Chinese Reception: The overseas Chinese gave the representatives from various parts of China a very warm reception. A reception committee was organized, and individuals and various organizations held banquets for the representatives in shifts. The Consulate General and the Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from Shanghai stating that a large number of tourist groups from China had left Shanghai on the night of the 19th. They consulted with the Philippine conference and the Carnival Organizing Committee for a grand welcome. (Sent by Yan Wenchou)

Ministry of Education's National Language Unification Society Promotes National Language Shorthand in Shanghai 174

Establishment of a Branch Institute for National Language Shorthand Instruction

Since 1929, the National Language Unification Preparatory Committee of the Ministry of Education has established the National Language Shorthand Training Institute in Beiping, using the Wang Yi-style method, and has held more than ten sessions. In 1933, a branch institute was established in Nanjing, with a large number of students. In May 1933, Wu Zhihui conducted a long recitation experiment at the institute in Beiping, averaging more than 160 words per minute. In December of the same year, Zhao Yuanren conducted a short-term experiment at the institute, reaching 200 words per minute, demonstrating the speed and agility of the method. Now, for the convenience of comrades in Shanghai who wish to learn, the society has obtained approval from the Ministry of Education to establish a branch institute in Shanghai. The address of the institute is at the Municipal He'an Elementary School on Xinzha Road, and Wang Gongxia will be in charge of opening the class. Wang is the nephew of Wang Yi and has been studying Wang-style shorthand for more than ten years, with extensive experience. Registration has now begun.

The Municipal Education Bureau issued Notice No. 29130 on education matters yesterday regarding the distribution of funds for December to various social education institutions and municipal schools. Change of Director at Jinan University Affiliated High School 176

The National Jinan University Affiliated High School has a large number of overseas Chinese students, and its management is very conscientious. This semester, due to Principal Shen's busy schedule, he was unable to take care of the position of High School Director. He initially requested Liao Yunpeng to take over. However, Liao declined repeatedly due to his numerous affairs in Shanghai. After Principal Shen repeatedly urged him to stay, he reluctantly agreed to transfer the position to Liu Zhenru, Director of the Department of History and Geography of the university. Liu has been involved in education for many years and has extensive research on secondary education. Zhong Wanru was specially invited to serve as the Director of Academic Affairs. Ms. Zhong graduated from National Sun Yat-sen University and Guangdong Higher Normal School, and has served as the principal of Guangzhou Normal School, the principal of Shantou Municipal Girls' Middle School, the director of the affiliated high school and elementary school of National Sun Yat-sen University, the Director of Moral Education of Guangdong Provincial Girls' Normal School, and a member of the Preparatory Committee of Lingdong University. She has a wealth of experience in secondary education. Liu and Zhong both assumed their positions at the school yesterday.

Jian Guo Highschool invites Hu Puan to lecture. 177

Yesterday at this city’s Zhabei district, Jian Guo Highschool invited prominent scholar Hu Puan to come to the school and lecture on “Issues of National Studies” during the weekly memorial service for Sun Yat-Sen. Mr. Hu first discussed the meaning and scope of national studies, then focused on the category of national literature within national studies, briefly listing the types of national literature, roughly divided into three categories: (1) academic literature, (2) artistic literature, and (3) applied literature. Academic literature and artistic literature can be combined, so in practice there are only two types: artistic literature and applied literature. The methods of artistic literature are divided into four types: (1) entrusting objects, (2) leaving words, (3) creating sentences, and (4) using sounds. The methods of applied literature are divided into two types: (1) fairness and fluency, and (2) neatness and conciseness. With extensive evidence and both serious and humorous tones, the audience was moved. The lecture lasted for two hours.

Yesterday, at the Chinese Stock Exchange, the market initially remained swirling and firm, but suddenly turned to a rising trend in the afternoon. Flour, Wheat, and Bran Follow Exchange Rate Trends

After the opening of the flour market yesterday morning, prices for imported wheat were quoted lower, with Chicago down about 0.22-0.23 yuan and Canada down about 0.40 yuan. In the afternoon, the rebound in the flour market and the sharp rise in gold prices led to temporary short covering, causing a strong rally in the market. Future price movements will continue to depend on exchange rate fluctuations. As a result, March/April rose by 0.10 yuan, and August rose by 0.09 yuan. Spot wheat is scarce, with few deliveries reported.

Free Talk

Art and Life 183

— Ren

Not long ago, there was a discussion on "Writers and Life." Opinions were divided into three schools: one advocated that writers must participate in life as writers; one advocated that writers must participate in life as ordinary people; and the other believed that the quality of a writer's work had nothing to do with the richness of life, but depended entirely on the richness of the writer's imagination. These three schools can actually be divided into two different principles. The first and second schools recognize that writers must enrich their lives. The third school denies that writers must enrich their lives; that opinion is quite grand and need not be discussed. But which of the first and second schools is correct? We can refer to the words of Guyau for reference.

In his book "Art from a Sociological Standpoint," Guyau has a chapter discussing "The Expression of Individual and Social Life in Art," saying:

"The true artist, rather than qualifying as an artist, should regard events as a member of humanity, a philanthropic person in society. Otherwise, a person carrying this duty (that is, a person who considers himself an artist) is killing his emotions in his heart and taking away the life that is the real foundation of true beauty from his work. "A person who sees nothing but art in his eyes often only perceives what is easily expressed by art in his life itself, and what is easily transferred to the false world. And he tends to abandon other things. Such a person often gradually invades the scope of real life with art. His emotion is often combined with this practical purpose and with his own artistic interest. He no longer feels for the sake of feeling, but feels for the sake of using or transferring his emotion. This is the same as an employee who works in business, whose words and deeds have lost their automatic nature and only know how to respond to things..." (According to my own "poor translation," Dajiang version)

Guyau is an advocate of art that should "express all the forces of life." So he: "Believes that life itself is important." He believes that before using things to express, you must "first feel what you feel." Otherwise, "you only see what can be obtained and captured, what can be expressed; as a result, you are obsessed with the superficial aspects of things. It is confusing nature with the museum." I think this opinion is generally agreeable. Of course, we ordinary people do not have such sublime reveries to talk about the philosophy of life with Guyau. But I always think that no matter who has artistic achievements, it is not as good as having achievements in life. Artistic achievements, in this period, are the greatest tragedy in life; and being able to achieve something in life, in any case, increases the driving force of historical progress.

I think the important thing now is not the writer and life problem. It is how our youth can enrich meaningful lives and how to live seriously. From the perspective of literature and art, it is only with a sincere life that there can be sincere literature and art. We must understand this.

Woven Eyes Beach 184

— Hei Ying

It was Tao, my former classmate, who knew my thirst for the sea, and tried every means to notify me after deciding the date of the woven-eye sea bath. So two days earlier, I returned to Medan from my aunt's house, gathered my fellow travelers, prepared picnic food on a very bright day, and set off in that big clumsy car.

"I've never been to Woven Eyes," I said to Tao in the car.

Tao patiently told me what kind of place it was. He also said that Woven Eyes is famous for sea bathing. Yes, there are really not many places to play on the huge island of Sumatra. I hoped that the sea of Woven Eyes could satisfy me.

After the car left the city, the road began to curve. On both sides are coconut groves or orchards planted with many different fruit trees. I poked my head out, and Malay villages also appeared, with some shirtless women feeding their livestock. The children shouted loudly when they saw our car approaching. Then it gradually became desolate. After crossing a stone bridge, Tao said that not far ahead was a small town, and asked if everyone wanted to stop and rest for a while. But everyone was eager to bathe, so no one advocated stopping. In this way, the car rushed through the small town and drove straight to its destination.

It takes about two hours to get from Medan to Woven Eyes. However, the beach is half an hour away from Woven Eyes; so, after taking a slight breath in Woven Eyes, we hurried on the road again.

"It's really far!" someone said.

However, precisely because the journey was too long, the joy in everyone's heart was doubled on their faces when they arrived at their destination. The car stopped, and we all jumped down and walked to the beach. Tao meant to eat first and then play; the two female companions were obviously also hungry and immediately expressed their consent. And I, with Xuan and Shun, acted alone. I changed into my swimsuit and jumped into the sea. The sea of Woven Eyes is boundless, rolling up white waves, sometimes crashing onto the beach. Immersed in the salty seawater, with the equatorial noon sun overhead; at this time, everyone forgot the heat and enjoyed everything the sea had to offer. The wind was blowing, and the coconut groves by the sea were roaring. Tao was calling us to eat, so I walked ashore wet and had our picnic under a small pavilion made of palm leaves.

"It's not easy to get together!" Shun said, biting a chicken leg, "We should have a good time today."

Yes, after eating, I rested in the pavilion, while they went back to the sea. This was the time of high tide, and the turbulent sea water rushed towards the beach, majestic and great. "I forgot to bring my camera!" I muttered to myself. I didn't know that Tao had already used his camera to take pictures of his female companions.

"Take one for me too!" I walked over, stood on the beach, and the knee-deep seawater kissed my ankles intimately. Behind me was the vast sea. ...

Now, three years later, I turned out this photo taken at the Woven Eyes beach from the corner of the box, and looking at the faded appearance, I felt that time had passed quickly, and I was much older. Having tasted the bitterness of wandering and the hardships of life, on a slightly old heart, recalling those playful days, I couldn't help but sigh.

Memories of a Terrifying Life (Part 1) 185

— Lan Ru

1918 was an unprecedented year of calamity for the people of Anhua and Xinhua counties. From spring to autumn, they endured eight months of terror. Farmers working in the fields were captured by the Northern Warlord army to serve as porters. If they tried to escape, they were shot immediately. If they walked too slowly due to carrying heavy loads, their legs were stabbed with bayonets. At night, these prisoners were locked in a dark room without food or permission to go outside to urinate. Many who dug through the walls to escape were caught and killed, and their tattered clothes were stripped off their corpses by the soldiers to be used as bundles.

Women living by the roadside were rarely spared from rape. Eighty-year-old grandmothers and eleven- or twelve-year-old girls were raped to death in unknown numbers! After looting the homes of the slightly wealthy, they would kill the occupants. The poor had even their sweet potatoes stolen. They fired their guns everywhere they went, looting everything. After looting the cities, they would march in teams with their guns to the countryside for more looting, indiscriminate killing, kidnapping, and arson...

The climax was the bloodbath of Lantian, where corpses piled up like mountains, blood flowed like rivers, and houses were burned to the ground, leaving only cries and a scene of unspeakable tragedy...

The origin of this disaster was as follows:

The Northern Warlord Zhang Jingyao and the Southern Tan Haoming were sworn enemies. In the first Northern and Southern War, the North won and the South lost. As a result, Zhang's army passed through Changsha and went directly to Xinhua and Baoqing. Stationed in Xinhua was the Fifth Regiment, whose commander was Zhang Jingyao's adopted son, named Zhang Jizhong. The soldiers of this regiment were all like bandits, engaging in rape, looting, killing, and arson, so everyone called him the "Rotten Fifth Regiment."

One day, more than twenty soldiers passed through Xieduo Mountain (my hometown, located between Xinhua and Anhua counties, which people traveling between the two counties or from Changsha had to pass through). They ate food and wore straw sandals at a shop without paying. When the shopkeeper asked for payment, they not only refused but drew their bayonets to threaten him, shouting, "Hmph! How dare you ask me for money? Be careful of your dog's life!" With that, they ran away. The shopkeeper was furious and gathered more than twenty people to chase after them. The soldiers raised their guns (luckily, they were guns without bullets). The crowd shouted loudly, and men, women, old, and young all ran out to chase the Northern soldiers. Some threw stones at them, some used kitchen knives to slash at them, and even children were hitting and yelling with small sticks. As a result, in Qingfeng Bridge, several Northern soldiers were beaten to a bloody pulp by the crowd. The crowd was overjoyed, jumping and shouting, "Good job, beat them hard! We will beat these bandits who harm the people to death one by one."

The next day, an order came from the regimental headquarters stating that the incident yesterday was serious. Not only were they to arrest the murderers, but they were also to burn down the entire village of Xieduo Mountain. The shopkeeper who caused the trouble, named Xie Chengkun, was an honest and capable middle-aged man who often visited my family. After receiving this news, he rushed to ask my father to find a way to resolve the situation. My father knew that this matter was too serious, so he had to invite many elders to go to the county to negotiate. At the same time, he led more than two hundred men and women, old and young, into the city to "cry injustice," explaining that yesterday's incident was not the people beating the soldiers, but the soldiers beating the people.

Who knew that once they arrived in the county, my father and all those who went with him were detained. At this time, the entire county was in an uproar. Everyone said that the Northern Warlords were unreasonable. If they did not release the petitioners and withdraw the order to burn down Xieduo Mountain, they would fight to the death. At this time, the bravery of the people of Xieduo Mountain and their iron-clad solidarity had already made the commander of the Rotten Fifth Regiment tremble. Coupled with the petition of 40,000-50,000 people from the entire Xinhua County, he was even more frightened out of his wits. Early the next morning, he released all the arrested people and appointed my father as a "High Advisor" (naturally, the title was completely nonsensical!). My father knew that this was too ridiculous. He was a noble recluse, and now his name was listed in the ranks of the warlords, which was indeed an insult. However, in order to protect the lives of the people in his hometown, he had to endure the humiliation and accept the letter of appointment.

After a period of peace, the farmers all thanked my father, but in fact, this was achieved by their own strength.

The war between the North and the South never stopped. Finally, the Southern army won and the Northern soldiers retreated. Then they remembered the hatred of a month ago. On the 120-li stretch from Xinhua to Anhua, they killed anyone they saw and burned every house they came across. It was early September, and the farmers had harvested their crops, but all the grain locked in the warehouses was burned. The houses became piles of rubble, and those who did not escape could not even find their bones. Those who escaped and returned were filled with sorrow, their wives and children scattered, and they had no desire to live. Several families in Lantian stayed in their houses because they had too many belongings and were afraid of being robbed. Who knew that the fire would come and turn their bones into charcoal. The two sons of Xie Yutongheng (the only shop that delivered messages for my family) were burned to death, each leaving behind a young and beautiful wife who was several months pregnant. When they heard that their husbands had been burned to death, they immediately went to drown themselves in the river, but luckily they were seen and rescued. Later, both of them went blind from crying.

Street Woman 186

— Ye Yin

Did she want to do it herself! —

However, A Xiang finally became a street woman.

Natural disasters and man-made disasters merged into a black tide of rural bankruptcy,

A Xiang was also one of those washed to Shanghai by this black tide;

At first, she thought, Shanghai was a place made of gold,

From now on, maybe she wouldn't have to cry from cold and hunger anymore

But, who knows, the iron hammer of reality,

Would shatter her dreams all at once! —

Yes, A Xiang also has strength, and A Xiang is also willing to endure hardship;

But can you tell her where the employer is, west or east?

She also sat in a job introduction office for more than a month,

But she wore out her ass and rarely anyone came to ask;

She also ran all over the silk factories and yarn factories,

But either they were reducing workers, or preparing to close down.

Finally, disappointment filled A Xiang's heart,

Several times she intended to throw herself into the Huangpu River;

But she stopped temporarily,

Because she remembered her weak younger brother and old mother in her hometown who were suffering from hunger and cold.

So, A Xiang finally became a street woman. —

However, did she want to do it herself!

Towards Evening (14) 187

— Qu Yi

The prisoners and the women seemed frightened by the solemn atmosphere and dared not act recklessly for a moment. However, the wheezing sounds from those smoking opium in the bunks, like chewing on rubber candy, seemed to invigorate the intruders.

"Oh my! So, young master Hu is no longer a brigade commander!" A woman with a Guanyin-like face and large buttocks immediately rushed to the bunk! "You're putting on airs." She also spoke in a mixed and awkward Shanghai dialect.

Putting down the opium pipe, he embraced the large buttocks around the waist. "We're old friends, come on, darling, play a tune to cheer me up! Let you, along with the 'Red Head' writer, perform a night battle at Ox Head Mountain, to gain some prestige!"

"Pah! Be careful not to twist your mouth!" Pushing him away, the large buttocks stood up again. Looking outside the cave entrance, beside the two drunk men lying on their backs, each had already sat up with two "female comrades." And the drunk men were actually moving their hands and feet, doing something unknown. Only the new literary figure was still shaking his head frequently in the corner of the room.

Afterwards, he also got up. The author of "New Literary Grand View" wanted to take a bath. It seemed that his whole body had been dirtied by the air in this room, and he had to scrub it clean with soap. But just as he was about to walk towards the bathroom, a shout came from the bunk.

"Old Guo! Come here! Come here!" The voice was clearly Hu Yiyuan's. "I'll introduce you to a friend, a friend—"

Without hesitation, he turned around. Old Guo entered the bunk.

The scene in the bunk at this time was: a male couple lying horizontally on the bed, and a female couple sitting quietly beside the bed, each stroking the man's legs. Four pairs of dark eyes, like four pairs of silver handcuffs, held Old Guo's limbs stiff.

"Let me introduce you," Hu Yiyuan said, waving his opium pipe, "This is the only writer in Hankou."

"Um!" Upon hearing the word "writer," he couldn't help but feel angry. He himself had written millions of words, but had not yet obtained this title. Now Hu Yiyuan was actually easily placing this laurel on this person's head. It was as if he was demoting himself to a third-rate writer. It was a bit like "mother's something". However, he couldn't do that, he still had to learn from Sakyamuni's obedience. He grunted an "Um".

"Hee—" The man on the other side stood up, took off his bird-shaped hat, and displayed his head under the interplay of the opium lamp and electric light. Smooth and glowing, rosy and slightly milky white, the man nodded as if deliberately showing his admirable head to the new literary figure. He immediately lay back down, and went back to talking his own talk.

"Honestly, there's one more thing—that, that Pacific Hotel side, is waiting for you... I thought, you—even if you don't want this share—this share of fifty yuan a month allowance. What is it really to you? But, but, that is what we newspaper conmen—ah, it's what the people who run the newspaper deserve. After all, we—we are still running such a big newspaper. And you, and you have put in some capital. Some people, humph, usually, usually don't publish the newspaper. Don't publish the newspaper, and when it comes to the end of the month, wanting to get a free salary, then, then overnight, overnight rush to print half a page of fart text, claiming to be, also claiming to be a small newspaper. Fifty yuan—fifty yuan, they still have to take it"!..."

Supplement of Local News from Shen Bao

Random Talks

How Magnificent, The "Black Hero"! 188

— Xing An

The dispute between Italy and Abyssinia has now lasted for two months, and there is still no proper way to resolve it. It seems that war is probably unavoidable. We don't need to worry about that. In any case, big countries bullying small countries is a matter of course in the current world. There's nothing strange about that. What we want to bring up here is this: An American famous black aviator, Colonel Julian, this time seeing the conflict between Italy and Abyssinia, was aroused by a kind of enthusiasm for protecting his race. He specially led fifteen pilots from New York to Africa on the twenty-second of last month, intending to help Abyssinia and fight against Italy when the conflict is resolved and war begins. According to Julian, Abyssinia is the only surviving empire of black people. If a war breaks out, all black people in the United States are willing to participate in the war to defend this country.

This is obviously a heroic act! Abyssinia is a small country, and Italy is a big country. For a small country like Abyssinia to confront a big country like Italy is like an egg hitting a stone. The success or failure of the war can be predicted in advance. However, Abyssinia refuses to overestimate its own strength and is unwilling to show weakness. It grits its teeth and wants to fight Italy! Abyssinia is fighting for its national dignity. It is excusable to use the country's entire military force to resist a strong enemy out of necessity. What is surprising is that this "black hero" Julian, who lives far away in the United States, could not bear to see Italy being too powerful. He was stirred by his enthusiasm for protecting his race, and specially led fifteen warriors from New York to Africa to prepare to participate in the war, to help the Abyssinian of the same race to resist the Italian of a different race. This is truly a rare and heroic act!

Julian is not a fool. He himself knows that his strength is very weak and is not enough to save Abyssinia. However, he is determined, fearless, and wants to go to the front line to fight against the strong enemy. Why is this? For nothing else, but to protect his race! Because he protects his race, he is willing to sacrifice for his race and disregard life and death!

Only with Julian's ambition can he be called a "national hero!"

Fresh Snow After a First Clearing 189

— Hu Weixiong

It had been snowing for several days, and it wasn't that I didn't have the refined interest in searching for plum blossoms in the snow, but unfortunately, the old lady was a particularly strong conversationalist. She specially lit a brazier for me in the study, and from morning to evening accompanied her grandson to chat. Even meals were brought in by Aunt Huang. She said that on snowy days, she often chanted scriptures alone by the brazier. In the past, there was also a pet cat that hid in her arms and pretended to chant scriptures. That feeling was strangely relaxing, but a little lonely. It meant that having guests to chat with for a long time was something she couldn't ask for more. Fortunately, I also had this skill, and could talk about anything in a coherent way, passing the three days of flying heavy snow.

Today, pale yellow sunlight has already crept onto my writing desk. I pushed open the long windows that had been tightly closed for three days. The courtyard was filled with three inches of silver-like snow. Except for the passageway in the middle for going in and out, I took a deep breath of the cold air, and my mind became clear. For recuperating from illness, I think traveling is the best method, because no matter the grass or trees, changing the environment makes everything feel unexpectedly intimate. However, for people like me who exchange our bodies for bread, it is difficult to find this kind of opportunity.

After breakfast, I searched out a hiking stick from my luggage and, with the old lady's permission, took her seven-year-old grandson as a companion for my first outing to the countryside.

The sky after the snow had cleared was bright and clean, and the world before my eyes was like a brocade embroidered with silver. Placed in such a scene, walking felt somewhat light and ethereal. My friend's home is a remote, isolated village. After the fresh snow, the road wasn't muddy. The child probably rarely had the opportunity to go out, and he always stayed ten paces ahead of me. As we walked along, I couldn't help but feel a surge of refined poetic inspiration.

However, that was just wishful thinking. It was difficult to recite the works of previous generations, and my own ability to make nonsense was useless. But it was already satisfying enough to randomly string together nonsense rhymes. And many fantasies surged into my heart. If I were riding a donkey and the child were a young servant, wouldn't that be full of poetry even if I couldn't find traces of plum blossoms?

The countryside has many trees, and the bare branches are piled high with thick snow. Occasionally, a few sparrows looking for food would perch on them. The snowflakes that the branches shook off when startled looked like fountains from a distance. —In the hands of a poet,

Page 19

, it would be like the Yellow River flowing from the sky. However, I am not a poet, and this scenic spot is not found among the famous places in China. Exaggerated descriptions would be seen as the ravings of a madman. To be selfish, Hangzhou, where grass grows in Jiangnan, gathers people from all directions, and you can't find a clean piece of land in West Lake. I hope that this complete piece of land in a remote corner will not suffer that kind of cruel trampling!

Walking windingly along the small path, I was blocked by a clear stream. Peering forward through the dense jungle, it probably doesn't end here. Scenic spots often have the temptation of prominent peaks. However, the child was not a thorough guide, and I was a stranger. When I felt a little tired, I brushed off the snow and sat down on a white stone to rest.

The stream had frozen, and the snow on the north side had not melted. The reeds along the river bank stretched, and the snow layer and the light of the sun formed a spectacular headdress. At this time, I regretted that I had forgotten to bring a camera. Otherwise, I should have let my friends who miss my condition taste my leisurely joy and congratulate me; moreover, this rare opportunity is about to be lost in an instant, although perhaps it provides me with a more unrestrained appearance!

Unintentionally throwing a small stone, three or five wild ducks flew out of the reeds in a panic, without any direction. The nearby snowflakes were all dissolved in the clear stream. I regretted doing something sinful. The wonderful scene that was about to be lost was played by me as a cruel executioner! I couldn't let go of it for a long time, and I no longer had the intention to explore the secrets in front of the jungle! (Random Notes on Rural Life, Part 3)

A Day Trip to Kunshan 190

— Ronin

As soon as the train arrived at Kunshan Station, the pointed pagoda on Kunshan Hill appeared in sight. Walking over the overpass on the tracks, squeezed into the crowd, a stone road was laid out in front of us between the bare trees of winter.

Kunshan City, like all old Chinese cities, is crowded with narrow roads and small houses.

Hiring rickshaws to guide us, we were brought to the tomb of Gui Youguang. A stone tablet and a round mound marked the resting place of this great writer of the Ming Dynasty. The place was desolate and not worth seeing. For us young people, who had no nostalgia, we decided to go elsewhere after a glance.

Only the old tomb gate remains in my memory.

We ate lunch at a restaurant. The four round tables were bustling with excitement, filling up with our group of young people. Young people have active hearts, and they became unrestrained after a few cups of Lao Hua Diao wine. Women often play a role in groups, and rosy cheeks often stir the entire group into a chorus of cheers.

After the meal, we took a car to Ma'anshan. The long stone steps softened our legs, which were used to living on flat ground. When we reached the top of the mountain, everyone couldn't help but take a breath. The wooden fish sounded loudly in the ancient temple, and the monks were chanting scriptures. The abbot placed us in a small meditation hall, but the Zen flavor couldn't contain the wild hearts of these young people, so they started playing the game of drawing lots in front of the Buddha. When a certain gentleman and a certain lady drew the best lots, a burst of cheers celebrating the success of their love was shouted out.

Looking down from the top of the mountain, the entire Kunshan and a vast plain came into view. Like Chairman Lin who toured Kunshan, we also took photos in front of the temple.

We rested at Banyuan Garden. The young people hurriedly carried cameras, hunting for scenery everywhere, capturing them into their lenses. The yellow flowers had withered, and Banyuan Garden couldn't keep our footsteps.

From the Kunshan Library, we retrieved Gu Yanwu's handwriting. We had paid attention to this late Ming Dynasty pragmatist's book on the advantages and disadvantages of prefectures and kingdoms during the national crisis. However, Gu Yanwu had died, and the times were no longer the times of the ancients. Besides being once captured by the camera, the book on the advantages and disadvantages of prefectures and kingdoms probably had little value.

It was already dusk, and we walked back to Kunshan Station on the narrow and rugged stone road. The bare branches were gradually covered with evening smoke, and the station was crowded with figures again.

A certain Mr. carried a duck breast and pastries, and another Mr. joked:

"Wasn't the duck noodles at noon enough?"

"Is it for—?" another Mr. said.

A burst of laughter erupted.

The ladies were so bored waiting for the train that they started playing at the station. They attracted the attention of all the guests, stretching out the necks that had shrunk in winter.

The train started. The fields were ruled by the night. Except for the lights on the train, the surroundings were completely dark.

The bright lights indicated the arrival of Shanghai. After a day of separation, seeing the lights made us feel happy; and the day trip to Kunshan was thrown to the back of our minds.

Notes of a Shell Collector 191

— Xu Xizhen

The February wind came rolling like a flywheel; in the fields and on the beaches, a kind of naturally hinted sound was faintly floating; like poetry, like pastoral songs, like the whisper of a six-stringed instrument:

"In the season when the north wind subsides, the wind on the beach has a sweet taste, the ice cubes disappear in the water, but green grass grows on the mud."

The call of spring, like a morning bell, leisurely broke the dreams of the shell collectors who had been hibernating for a winter.

So I got up and cast a surprised glance at the outside world again: the seasons don't know how to lie; really, the ice cubes had disappeared on the water surface, and the wind on the sea no longer had the harsh salty sharpness: the sky was crystal blue, bright, and vast. Two or three seagulls flew up on the beach. The world was quiet, ambiguous, and people's hearts were endlessly open.

I also cast a friendly greeting at the sea, and forgot all the hatred of the dangerous waves of the previous night - the sea is the greatest, it is the sky of the ground, stretching with boundless vastness, and it is difficult for people to measure its end.

I must be grateful that spring has brought us the "Mother Sea" of Xu Cixiang again, and looking at her, we have a younger posture, and green endless waves.

So I faced the sun - the sun that had just appeared on the horizon, took a deep breath of vitality, and began to use my spirit to deal with the waves that were galloping in the arms of the sea - they were like light cavalry in the desert, and like soldiers on the fire line, relentlessly one walking in front of the other, and then swallowing the one in front.

The sumo of the giant waves gave me a new chill.

However, terrifying waves are very common for shell collectors. In order to find some permanent and precious things, in a series of mornings and evenings, they brave the wild and violent tides and fearlessly plunge into the dangerous waves: the body is involuntarily pushed by a kind of great force, and even I don't know where it will be pushed; so: I abandon the world's worries, abandon the vague fate, and put all the instinct of survival on one goal: to pick up those crystal clear shells, in which there is an unknowable existence of a kind of light, a kind of treasure, a kind of dazzling pearl.

It is this kind of great purpose that can make a young shell collector forget the emptiness of the sea, the great power of the tide, and the danger of the waves: let me pick up those bright things; otherwise, let me be swallowed by the waves.

So, long days came and passed; but the shell collector kept fighting the terrifying waves and sucking the salty wind; the heart was terrified, but in this terror, how much kindness and expectation existed?

So one day finally came: in the immeasurable shells, a pearl was shining, dazzling the eyes of the shell collector, and also boiling the moving heart of the shell collector.

Thinking over and over again: "Is it a dream or reality?"

Understood: it is reality; but this reality is: efforts and brave seeds are sown in the ideal.

Even if it is said that the shell collector has the loneliness of a wanderer and the roughness of a fugitive; but I know, clearly know: one day, he will also raise a poetic smile.

In front is the boundless sea, and the rolling waves, but it has long been said that terrifying waves are not unusual for shell collectors. For the achievement of a greater ideal, I finally swam once again to the boundless terrifying waves.

I advise you all to happily put down your opium pipes, put down your opium pipes and the country will be strong. A sallow and thin face is truly bitter. A bent back and waist is not a good look. Yao Xiao'an Wang Pingqiu Qilin Leopard

Opening Chapter "Great Bargain"

This year's famine has made everything withered, and the market business is desolate. Goods are piled up like mountains in the store, with various colors shining high. I only see the shop assistants idle to read the newspaper, from morning to night it is really boring. If you expect the business situation in the city to be good, you must hope that the farmers will harvest. If the farmers can have a bumper harvest and the people are happy, the transaction will naturally be lively. If the countryside is going bankrupt, where will the surplus funds come from to buy light silk? Therefore, businessmen have no choice but to think hard and break the boredom. I called a group of drummers to knock loudly on the door. Colorful flags were hung in front of the door, and electric lights shone brightly all night. The big characters clearly show the reduced price, marking the price of the reduced rate. It is true that as soon as you shout loudly, people will respond and rush to compete. Gold, pearls and diamonds are not asked, and rough cloth and foreign yarn are greatly sold. From this one end, we can see the general trend, and the countryside is indeed hungry and barren. If we do not think of a way, we will see a scorched village. What is the point of seeking wealth in the city? It is futile to reduce prices. It is necessary to know that reducing prices is an expedient measure, and the root cause should be treated first. The business will not be desolate when the period is full.

Shen Bao Local Supplement: Automobile Weekly

The Frenzy of British Car Manufacturers in Producing Sporting Automobiles 196

— Ying Dai

Pay attention to sporting automobiles – this can be said to be true. British car manufacturers, in the past, in terms of society, contributed vehicles solely for transportation purposes, neglecting everything else. They also didn't care about the value of the vehicles that car owners exchanged their money for. However, judging from the current situation, it is clearly different from the past. Each automobile exhibition shows us that the market for sporting automobiles has become unique and the value of the vehicles themselves is improving year by year. In this short article, to say that it can fully introduce the advantages of the 1935 British-made sporting automobiles to readers is certainly impossible. If you want to clearly distinguish between sporting automobiles and phaetons, it's even more difficult. At one time, everyone thought that those with hardtops were not new sporting automobiles. But this principle is now completely inapplicable. Especially since there are many serious dual-purpose sedans here that can have the spirit of sporting automobiles when driving.

Innovation in Manufacturing: If you want to buy an open-top car that isn't a sporting style, it's even more difficult. Although streamlined designs have long been used on non-open-top cars, they have also begun to be used on open-top cars. As for the body of a sporting car, generally speaking, there have been no major reforms compared to the 1934 model from a year ago. All the rain gear is less, and it is more hoped to be improved. Especially in convertibles with real hardtops, some rain gear, after being folded, can block the line of sight. Moreover, when the vehicle is driving, there are various unrestricted noises, and sometimes a piece of cotton cloth will be dragged down. Some new car bodies are heavier. Perhaps many car owners would rather sacrifice one or two miles per hour of speed because the heavier body is more stable when installed on the chassis. Some car factories, regarding the manufacture of car bodies, even for very small cars, now consider having a luggage rack at the rear for long-distance travel or long-distance racing applications. However, regarding this point, it also takes a lot of effort to manufacture. Some people even think that it's better to remove the spare tire than to put the luggage in a covered part.

Improvements in Driving Position: Especially for high-speed and semi-racing new cars, the space occupied by the seats this year has been improved compared to last year. Paying attention to the saying "If you want to drive a car quickly and safely, you should always see the two front wheels, if possible, always see them." Regarding this point, perhaps there are one or two small new cars that still need to be improved, but overall they are more advanced than last year. In addition, we have a method of analyzing new British-made sporting cars, which is based on the honors won in past automobile races. We must admit that there is a new car, the Delage Two-Liter Dolomite, which is a new car manufactured in Britain. When designing it, it was completely designed to be suitable for participating in new-style automobile races as a standard. However, it can also be used for other purposes at ordinary times. The new car has eight cylinders, using double overhead camshafts, driven by the center point of the entire cylinder. It has a good dry sump lubrication system and a beam-supported frame. The center of gravity is very low and it can travel 100 miles per hour. Secondly, there is a three-liter and a half six-cylinder Brough Superior, which is not expensive, but in automobile races, the speed can also reach 100 miles per hour. It is indeed a very beautiful new car. For those that can be used as both sedans or convertibles, the high-quality mixed gold mixed into the raw materials is not in the minority. There are, of course, many new cars from famous British-made sporting car manufacturers this year that will be contributed to us. What is especially noteworthy is the product of the MG factory. As a result of participating in automobile races on the Old Continent in the past, it has won many honors. Here, in various racing cars, we can find the Q-type MG 750cc four-cylinder new car, and the K3 Magna new car, which looks very much like a commercial vehicle. It has also won many honors in the UK. The two new cars mentioned above, in terms of speed, can travel two miles per minute. Other sporting cars include the S-type 750cc MG car, the Magna 1,100cc six-cylinder car, and the N-type 1,287cc six-cylinder Magna new car, etc. The S-type can travel 75 miles per hour, and the N-type can travel 80 miles per hour, both of which have very eye-catching open-top bodies mounted on them.

A Glimpse of Large Vehicles: In addition, there is another very prestigious British-made sporting car, the Talbot. On this new car, we can find a centrifugal clutch and an early-selection gearbox. The three-and-a-half-liter new car is manufactured very exquisitely, and the famous "95" and "105" models still have considerable achievements. The Olives 20 horsepower car has also been extremely popular in the past. The 1935 engine, which is 2,762cc, six-cylinder, still uses the multi-valve spring with a leading patent. The front wheels are independently suspended. Because of the excellent chassis, there are special achievements when driving. Among the phaetons, there is also a special achievement, the four-and-a-half-liter Lagonda car. Without increasing the price, the new Le Birt chassis is also an advanced product of engineering among British-made sporting cars that travel 100 miles per hour. The engine is a six-cylinder, 4,467cc SU carburetor two-seater, double ignition. This new car also has a special feature, namely the Clairense traffic jam system. The new three-and-a-half-liter new car is also an innovative product. The selling price is only 695 pounds. The small 1,104cc Le Bor four-cylinder car with double overhead camshafts is still a convertible. The Clifford 1,100cc new car can also be used as a racing car. It has already had significant achievements in the past.

康天寗及其他：Now I will describe the various new cars produced by Connaught. There are two types of Alfa Romeo cars, 19-63 horsepower and 19-76 horsepower, both of which are 2.2-liter, in-line eight-cylinder new cars. Although this new car is similar to the Ferrari giant car that travels 170 miles per hour, it travels very quickly and looks very much like a commercial sporting car. In addition, the appearance is even more beautiful. The streamlined sedan is even more famous. The 76-horsepower new car's engine speed has developed to 4,400 times per minute. It is also a double camshaft, and the engine crank rod has seven bearings. The Bok car, judging from the Olympia Motor Show, has been widely used in recent years. In the "57" model, there is a 33 model new car, which can use the highest gear for driving under any circumstances. It is very fast. Among the Mercedes new cars, there is a two-seater sporting new car equipped with a five-liter in-line eight-cylinder engine. The actual horsepower can reach 160 horsepower at its highest. It is also independently suspended on the front wheels. Most of the other vehicles exhibited at the conference focus on travel rather than sporting, and the 1,300cc rear-engine streamlined chassis is a new product of Mercedes. It has undergone a lot of consideration when manufacturing it.

Side-Valve New Car: In addition, there is also an Italian style, which can occupy a place in sporting cars, that is the QM new car. Perhaps the one using side-valve is this one. The OHV chassis is indeed very popular. The OM brand car is historically famous for using side-valve engines. Silent lubrication, easy acceleration, are all reliable in this six-cylinder engine. Among small cars, British products are better than others and have many characteristics that are praised by overseas countries. In the one-and-a-half-liter new car, there are two types of Flanshana Hiss and Aston Martin. They have both won supreme honors in automobile races. The former especially has special advantages, and the ratio of power and volume is unmatched by any vehicle. Aston Martin is usually low and smooth, very much like a commercial car. Hiss has four-cylinder and six-cylinder types (including the 1,657cc new car). The AM is a 1,496cc four-cylinder car with a camshaft. It especially uses a dry sump and double lubrication. The Lemans and TT types are even better products of this year.

Various Recent Products: The British Salmon, this name, follows Aston Martin. It is an old-fashioned and well-manufactured chassis. The horsepower is only 17-70 horsepower. It is the most fashionable four-seater convertible. The most beautiful 1935-style sporting new car in appearance is the AC Ace. It has six cylinders, 1,900cc, overhead camshaft, and three carburetors. It is a very neat four-seater sporting car. On the body of this new car, there is also a luggage compartment attached. Among Austin cars, the most famous is an improved "65" style sporting new car, equipped with a two-seater 7 horsepower chassis. In addition, there are three British-made new cars that are worth remembering. They are Leland, Delage, and Star. The first one has had amazing achievements in racing competitions in the past. This year, it still maintains this advantage. Among them, there is also a one-and-a-half-liter four-cylinder Lynx four-seater body and a fifteen horsepower MPH two-seater body, which are the neatest vehicles among current sporting cars. The 9-horsepower four-cylinder Imp new car has a short wheelbase. Its reputation is no less than Connaught. The Delage Dolomite car has already been mentioned above. In addition, there is a Crowla four-cylinder or six-cylinder car and a South Cross two-seater new car. The new-style Crowla car has now been increased to 1,232cc. There are two types, the base model and the Weathers model. The camshaft used in the latter is manufactured more specially.

Star's Attention to Convertibles: Star has been improving in the manufacture of sporting cars in recent years. It has now established its position. The 1935 new car includes the Liman 9 horsepower chassis and a Limant speed new car. It has a three-carburetor six-cylinder, one-and-a-half-liter engine. Among the products of the Hillman factory, the new car with the small Treasure four-cylinder, 1,185cc engine can reach a maximum of 70 horsepower.

Mallory's Sporting Car: The Mallory factory also has a very neat sporting new car this year, mounted on the "10-6" chassis. It has a double carburetor, 1.378-liter, six-cylinder engine. The results of the tests on this new car have proven that it is the most comfortable and best-performing new car among convertibles. The high-speed fourteen Zheng Luofer four-seater convertible is even a stunning new car. Its speed is unprecedented. The special seat of the Lyleton new car is curved. Its speed and beautiful appearance are also representative vehicles. In addition to the various sporting cars mentioned above, there are many other famous new cars that have crossed the Atlantic and sold overseas, such as the British-made new-style sporting cars, such as Rolls-Royce, Sunbeam-Talbot, and heavy cars such as the 100-mile-per-hour Trakia, Aston-Martin, Delahaye, Hispano-Suiza, Isotta Fraschini, and Hotchkiss, etc. The small Belilla Fasha car is a typical Italian product. In the past two years, the achievements of this vehicle have already been proven by racing competitions. It is also an overhead valve, 995cc, four-cylinder engine. It moves very smoothly. The fastest time can reach 80 actual horsepower. In short, all 1935-style sporting cars have made amazing progress, which is enough to prove the strong interest of British factories in manufacturing sporting cars.

Our local Hozing Motor Company has now shipped a large batch of 1935-style Oldsmobile cars. They are currently unpacking and assembling them. They will probably be officially displayed in the showroom the day after tomorrow. The picture shows a 1935-style Oldsmobile six-cylinder four-door sedan. The appearance is gorgeous and the interior is spacious. Six people can sit together and feel extremely comfortable. The front and rear seats have been widened. The motor and seats have been moved forward. All passengers are placed between the axles, making them feel more comfortable. As for the knee movements, they have been adopted as standard equipment for new cars.

Calculation Method of Air Resistance During Driving 197

— Zhenmin

When a car is driving, there is an invisible air resistance that prevents the car body from moving forward. This resistance increases with the speed of the car body. It is enough to reduce the engine's power and is an unavoidable loss in driving. But how big is this resistance? Although engineers from various countries have done many experiments before, such as wind tunnel

Page 24

experiments, etc., the results obtained cannot be accurately demonstrated.

We know that when testing in a wind tunnel, the car body is stationary, while the air is flowing. This is the opposite of the phenomenon during actual driving (during actual driving, the car body moves and the air is stationary). Therefore, the results obtained are not satisfactory. Later, some engineers put the car body on the car floor and isolated it with rollers. When the engine is running, the car body slides backward due to the action of air resistance. In this way, the relationship between air resistance and vehicle speed can be known. But the above methods are only to measure the approximate nature of this air resistance, and cannot absolutely know how much it is.

Until recently, an American engineering society invented an accurate on-site air resistance test. Its theory is very simple and interesting. It completely uses the inertia of objects to measure resistance.

When the car body accelerates forward, the people in the car will feel their bodies leaning forward. Conversely, when braking or decelerating, people's bodies will lean backward. Now, this new air resistance test is based on this principle. During the test, a special pendulum is hung on the side of the car body, allowing it to swing freely back and forth. Next to the pendulum, there is also a semi-circular scale. When the car body accelerates, the pendulum moves backward. When decelerating, it leans forward. The action is very sensitive.

During the test, first accelerate the car body to a certain level so that it does not change. Because of the action of air resistance, tire and engine resistance, the car body gradually slows down. At this time, the passengers in the car will absolutely not notice it, because this deceleration is very small. But this sensitive pendulum immediately shows the degree of deceleration of the car body. In this way, the total resistance on the car body, at any speed, can be read from the pendulum's scale. This scale directly marks the resistance unit of a few pounds per ton, which is very convenient to read.

The results of the test on a very long flat road show that the car body is first accelerated to 54 miles per hour. The scale reads 105 pounds per ton. When the speed is reduced to extremely slow (almost the same as walking) at 45 miles per hour, the table reads a record of 30 pounds (per ton). This record of 30 pounds is actually the pure "rolling resistance" of the wheels.

The record on the scale indicates the mixed resistance of air and wheels. But because the rolling resistance does not change at any speed, subtracting the rolling resistance of 30 pounds from each record will give you the air resistance (per ton). If the total weight of the car body in tons is known, then multiplying this tonnage by the air resistance per ton will give you the total air resistance.

The most accurate formula for calculating air resistance has now been determined by general engineers. For example,

F=KAY2 represents air resistance (per ton). A represents the area in front of the car (square feet).

V represents the speed per hour (miles). K is a constant that varies with the style of the car body. The more streamlined the car body, the smaller the value of K.

From the above formula, K can be read from the pendulum scale. A can be measured directly with a ruler. V can also be read from the speedometer. In this way, the value of K can be calculated very accurately. Its absolute value is roughly between 0.00175 and 0.00187. The following record is the result of a sedan test. The car body is five feet nine inches wide and five feet six inches high. The area in front of the car is twenty-six square feet. The car weighs 1.75 tons.

The most important result of this experiment is the measurement of K. Because after the value of K is measured, the air resistance at any speed can be calculated from the above formula. At the same time, the power lost due to air resistance can also be calculated from the speed and air resistance. This is really the most convenient thing.

According to multiple test results, the ideal value of K should be 0.0019 to 0.002. But because of various reasons, such as the speedometer's inability to be absolutely accurate, etc., the ultimate absolute value of K has not yet been determined. However, within the limits mentioned above, it can be safely used for generally streamlined car bodies now.

Hudson and Terraplane in 1935 198

— Ming

Since the Hudson Motor Car Company re-employed all its old staff, the manufacturing process has become more thorough and the production volume has increased accordingly. There is now talk of further expansion and recruitment of new staff. Work efficiency can be seen to have increased. The Hudson of 1935 has almost become the focus of attention of people all over the world. Its various astonishing records have made millions of people happy to use Hudson.

Everyone knows the effectiveness of the Terraplane automobile. The Terraplane Essek water car is also popular among the general public. The Terraplane record test is different from other automobile test methods. It is to seek its accuracy. The Terraplane automobile competition regulations formulated by the American Automobile Association Racing Department are unique. Its methods are accurate and without error. This shows that the performance of the Terraplane automobile is different from other automobiles.

The American Automobile Association's Terraplane automobile competition. Two Terraplane automobiles. Six self-stopping watches that have been calibrated by the standard timekeeping department are installed in a uniquely ingenious specialty. They can move or stop at the same time. After the six watches have been started, they are carried to the foot of the mountain. There are three timers there. They are given a running watch at the appropriate starting point for use in timing. The remaining three watches that are running at the same time are carried to the finish line of the competition on the mountain. There are also three timers there holding these three watches. After the car starts, the three watches at the foot of the mountain will stop. When they reach the finish line at the other mountain top, the three records at the finish line will also stop. The average of the three watches on each side is calculated to get two numbers. The difference between these two numbers is the time it takes for the car to travel in the middle. Its accuracy is guaranteed. Hudson automobiles have also had good records several times, and this has been even more comprehensively considered in the products of 1935. This method can be used to check the car's machinery at any time.

The Hudson Motor Car Company was founded in 1909. Among all the historical records of the Hudson Motor Car Company, there is a point about the Hudson automobile being happily used by the general public. According to detailed surveys, it is known that among all the vehicles sold by Hudson automobiles since it started business until now, more than 70 percent of them are still as good as new. These 70 percent of Hudson cars are still running on the market. The records also indicate the names, addresses and detailed usage of the customers who own these 70 percent of Hudsons. This is enough to prove that the products of Hudson automobiles are by no means ordinary automobiles that cannot withstand frequent use.

There is also a detailed report that there are now 1.5 million Hudson car owners in the Americas. The average car driver is satisfied with the effectiveness of the vehicles they have purchased and have used them for a long time. Nowadays, people no longer buy cars based on chance and neglect practicality. They must choose to purchase cars that have effective performance. The Hudson and Terraplane of 1934 have been praised by people. It can be expected that the Hudson and Terraplane of 1935 will be welcomed by people.

Shen Bao Local Supplement: Movie Supplement

A Brief History of the Development of Film (9) 200

— Wen Ying

(9) Charles Ray's Failed Change of Style

Working at the same studio as Nazimova at the same time was Rudolph Valentino. Besides him, there were also Ramon Novarro, Alice Jerry, Mae Murray, and others.

However, Charles Ray was the most popular male star at the time. He was originally a country boy, and the image he presented to the public on the screen was that of a quiet, shy, and timid young man. His success and popularity stemmed from this very trait. But after achieving success and enjoying fame, he decided to change his style. He wanted to discard his old straw hat, take off his worker's overalls, and put on regular clothes, acting like a social figure. Such changes in style are not uncommon in the history of cinema, but the success or failure of such experiments is extremely important to the future of a star, so we cannot help but discuss it in more detail.

Changing one's style is, at the very least, a risky endeavor. Because audiences are the absolute masters of the film industry, the quality of films and the rise and fall of stars all depend on the psychological support or opposition of the audience. This theory has been proposed before. Now, taking Charles Ray as an example, his success was due to the audience's fondness for his portrayal of a rustic young man, shy and retiring... just as later audiences enjoyed seeing Janet Gaynor's shy and quiet demeanor... If they don't like seeing you play a different style, no matter how tired you feel of your old style, no matter how well you think you can perform after changing your style, it will not be successful.

At that time, Charles Ray did not deeply understand the psychology of the audience, and the dictatorial authority of the audience. He decided to create a great and lasting work. To show his determination, he independently organized a company. He poured all his assets into that company, seriously wanting to bring a famous play (The Courtship of Miles Standish) to the screen. He not only put all his money into that endeavor, but also poured his entire spirit into it.

In order to make the film as accurate as possible, he hired several famous researchers and historians. Although it was a bold endeavor, Charles Ray believed that after future success, it would have indelible value in art. It is true that it had value in art, but when audiences saw Charles Ray wearing Puritan clothes, they were greatly disapproving and jumped up in objection. In this way, they lost the country boy they usually liked to watch, and they also didn't like the new style film.

The failure of this endeavor not only caused Charles Ray to lose the money he had accumulated over the years, but also caused him to lose the sympathy of the audience. Disappointed, he left the screen. After a few years, he joined MGM, wanting to resume his old career, but what he had lost was gone forever. In his new MGM film, he wore a top hat and a tuxedo, looking every bit the socialite. That film, called "Paris," also achieved considerable success, but not because of Charles Ray, but because of a new actress named Joan Crawford. "Paris" became a pivot of metabolism. The old struggled to return, and the new struggled to enter. Returning was not easy, but entering was successful. Now Joan Crawford has become a very popular star, but what about Charles Ray? He has now been reduced to an unknown bit part. The vicissitudes of life are truly felt.

From this, it can be seen that the film industry is mostly tied to the issue of people, and the product of the film industry is nothing more than the personality of people. Once that personality has been recognized by the audience, if an actor wants to change his inherent personality, nine times out of ten he will be hastening his own failure, because the audience's preconceived notions are already unbreakable. Janet Gaynor is a sweet and lovely woman, if she plays a worldly socialite, it will not suit the audience's taste. If Greta Garbo abandoned her mysterious cloak and actually played a lighthearted, humorous role, no matter how talented she was or how well she performed, the result would be a big joke.

Audiences have always been like this. They are still like this now. And they will always insist on their preconceived notions in the future. (To be continued)

Everything About "Resurrection" 201

— Huang Yingdai

Leo Tolstoy's masterpiece "Resurrection" has been brought to the screen by Rouben Mamoulian's production studio and distributed by United Artists. It will soon be shown at the Nanjing Grand Theater. In order to give readers a better understanding of the author, story, and main characters, I will describe them separately here.

(1) Author's Brief History Leo Tolstoy (1828-1910) was a Russian writer and religious thinker. His works had a considerable impact on the thinking of the modern literary world, not only in Russia, but arguably all over the world. Tolstoy completed three major masterpieces in his life: "War and Peace," "Anna Karenina," and "Resurrection." There are countless other works, both long and short, with translations in various countries. In terms of quantity, he can also be called the number one writer in modern literature. His life was a life of striving for the truth, from a life of the flesh to a life of the spirit. It was not until the age of fifty that he began to question life, and a major turning point occurred. The solution he found was in the Gospels of Israel, expressing the beliefs of primitive Christianity. "My Confession" was published because of this distress, and called out for non-resistance, non-property, pan-laborism, and fellow-citizenism, and acted from the standpoint of a religious thinker and social reformer. In his later years, in order to thoroughly change his life, he abandoned his beloved wife and became a monk, but died on the way, at the age of eighty-two.

(2) Story Summary "Resurrection" is a novel written by Tolstoy at the age of seventy, and is one of the three major masterpieces mentioned above. The film is titled "We Live Again Resurrection". The story tells of a prostitute, Maslova, who is suspected of murdering a customer and is detained for public trial. One of the judges in the public trial, Nekhlyudov, is greatly surprised when he sees her, because this woman is Katusha, a maid in his aunt's house. Ten years ago, when he was a young officer, he stayed at his aunt's house and seduced her. She became pregnant as a result, could no longer be a maid, and was abandoned by him, so she fell into prostitution. Nekhlyudov believed that her situation was all caused by him, so he wanted to save her and marry her to atone for his past sins. He went to see her in prison, but she no longer recognized him. Nekhlyudov then tried every means to rescue her, but the crime had already been decided, so he followed a team of prisoners to Siberia. At first, she scolded him, but later, seeing his sincerity, she was moved and gradually regained her original conscience, and did not want to marry him, so as not to hinder his path to happiness. Nekhlyudov also understood her good intentions and no longer pursued the matter. There was a political prisoner, Simonson, who knew that Katusha had changed her mind and wanted to marry her. Katusha was also interested in Simonson, so Nekhlyudov entrusted Katusha to Simonson, and he himself went on to engage in the great cause of saving all people. Tolstoy's final talk about saving society is to promote his great proposition, which in terms of thought, is the so-called Tolstoyism.

(3) Male and Female Leads Russian new star Anna Sten, in her Hollywood debut film "Nana", and her second film is starring in "Resurrection", playing the role of the maid Katusha, not only beautiful and moving, but also able to imitate the actions of her predecessors, playing a Russian peasant girl, full of emotions, and most appropriate. Fredric March's amazing performance in "The Royal Family of Broadway" has already received considerable evaluation, and in "Resurrection", he is the male lead, playing Nekhlyudov. What his achievements will be, we cannot judge before the performance, but in our expectation, he will not disappoint. During the filming of the entire film, the scenery and customs, etc., are all striving to be like real Russia, and have undergone considerable research beforehand.

Lianhua's New Film "Femme Fatale" Premieres Today 202

This year, Lianhua Film Company shocked the film industry with its two films "The Highway" and "New Woman". It also raised the banner of "Main Force Vehicles On the Move" and called for twelve major films. Looking at the listed productions, it is enough to show the consolidation and strength of its front, and looking around the film industry, there is almost no match for it. This is further evidenced by the film "Femme Fatale". The film's arguments are precise, alert and powerful, and the beauty lies in the fact that the plot is popular but does not fall into the usual stereotypes. The so-called beauty in the film is not originally a serpent, but unintentionally, often causes all kinds of sins, and its toxicity is even greater than that of a serpent. In this film, Zhang Yi indulges in female lust, abandons his wife and children, and when the spring dream wakes up, he is already bankrupt and his family is destroyed. Although this ending is not caused by himself, it cannot be blamed on the beauty. Zhang Yi uses his heroic personality to play the reckless man in the sea of desire. The scenes of repentance and madness show the maturity of his acting skills, and his great future is generally recognized by those who know him. Chen Yanyan plays the young woman, full of resentment and ends up depressed. Her performance is very vivid. Liang Saizhen's prostitute's movements do not flow into flirtation, but naturally have their touching points, and her steady work is unprecedented. The film's collaboration of the three, the sophisticated performances, and the good results are self-evident. Those who watched it yesterday praised it, which shows that public opinion is in the hearts of the people.

Pre-orders for The Great View of Chinese Movie Stars Begin 203

China's film industry has made significant progress in recent years. The directing techniques and the acting skills of the actors are no longer the same as in the previous period of film. Therefore, domestic films are emerging like a storm, and the screening period has broken the record in film history. In terms of art, it can also compete with famous Western films. Film artists are very popular with the public, and have gained a considerable position in society. Film publications have therefore been produced in large quantities, but there is a lack of reading materials that introduce the entire system of actors. In view of this, Yisheng Publishing House specially invited Chen Jiazhen, a photography expert active in the film industry, to edit "The Great View of Chinese Movie Stars", with pictures as the main body, and all those who appear on the screen are included, and all are specially photographed for this book. There are also rare film photos of historical value that are not seen outside. Most of the photos are taken by Chen himself, using the latest and most novel angles, and arranged and printed with the noblest paper materials. Its perfect results can be predicted, and pre-orders will begin soon.

Film Novel

Anecdotes of Wellington (The Iron Duke) (1) 205

— Xin Zhi

Produced by British Gaumont... Starring George Arliss

In the spring of 1815, peace returned to the European continent. The God of War stood high in the sky, overlooking the scarred earth, soaked in the blood of the men who had fought for twenty years. Now the sun and moon were shining again, and the five grains were growing again. The people were showing a bustling sound of coming and going, and the God of War could not help but snorted fiercely from his nose. He frowned and waited impatiently for his opportunity to spew out the fierce flames of destruction from his mouth to the human world again.

On the small island of Elba, south of the Italian coast, a man was standing on the rocky seashore, gazing sadly at the junction of the water and sky to the north, vaguely seeing his French homeland. He was Napoleon, the hero of the world. The angry tide hit the stones under his feet in waves, telling him that he had wings but could not fly. The eagle in the sky of the past was now in a cage.

Napoleon Bonaparte! For twenty years, his name had spread everywhere with the iron hooves of the army, and had been filled with the death and destruction of the dirge, and filled the world. He fought the world alone, and that world had once been in his grasp, but now that world, and all the enemies who combined to fight against him, had defeated him, imprisoned him, and exiled him to a small island in the Mediterranean Sea, letting him live and die on his own. He was that peace, how short-lived was that peace! The man standing on the seashore, although small in stature, had a heart of ambition that could not be caged like a beast. Moreover, his hometown was in sight, and his prestige had not completely disappeared. So after a few weeks...

In the palace of Vienna, the monarchs and dignitaries of various countries, a group of victors, were gathered to discuss how to divide the rich fruits of this victory. They were clamoring and fighting, and telling lies to deceive people, always wanting to get more than others. The King of Prussia was there, arrogant and tyrannical. He and the Austrian strategist Metternich, a gentle, polite, intelligent, and deeply prejudiced man, sat at one end of the conference table. There was also the French diplomat Talleyrand, who had once served as Napoleon's powerful minister, but now represented the Bourbon family, who had returned to the throne of France, at this historically famous Vienna Congress.

However, there was one person who did not clamor and roar like others. He sat quietly to one side, stretching out his legs comfortably, with a contemptuous smile on his face. That was the Duke of Wellington, who had led the allied forces to defeat Napoleon and help the Bourbon family to the throne. His reason for restoring the Bourbon family to the throne was not out of any preference for the Bourbon family. He felt that this was the only way to preserve the peace of Europe. As for the competition and greed of the people at the conference table, he felt it was extremely meaningless. His only task was to preserve the peace of Europe. The stability and prosperity of Europe was the happiness and satisfaction of England.

He sat quietly, lost in thought, but his thoughts were not on the clamoring and roaring of the King of Prussia, nor on Metternich's eloquent talk. What he was thinking about was outside the borders of Austria, surrounding the royal palace of Paris, France, sitting on the throne, was a fat, clumsy, and obsessed with the ancient ideas of royal power. But what he was thinking about was not Louis XVIII himself; next to that foolish and self-righteous monarch stood a woman, she was a beautiful woman, and her demeanor had once been the model of the French court. This woman, like so many women before her, wanted to manipulate the king and secretly become the master of France. (To be continued)
